Ka Seng Hynniewtrep Integrated Territorial Organization (HITO) ha ka 28 tarik Jymmang, ka la dawa na u Returning Officer ka Shillong Parliamentary Constituency uba dei ruh Deputy Commissioner ka East Khasi Hills District, u SC Sadhu ba u dei ban weng noh ia ka jingpynmih hukum ban pynjari da ka kyndon 144 CrPC ha baroh kawei ka district ha ka sngi niew vote na ka bynta ka Lok Sabha ilekshon kaba la dep ka ban long ha ka 4 tarik u Jylliew 2024.
Ha ka dorkhas sha u Deputy Commissioner u President ka HITO u Bah Donbok Dkhar u la ong ba kane ka hukum ba la pynmih ha ka 23 tarik Jymmang kaba la khanglad ia ka jingiaid rally da kin kino ki kyrtong ne party sain pyrthei hadien ba la pynbna ia ka result ka long pyrshah ia ka hok jong u paidbah kumba la kdew ha ka Article 14 bad 19 jong ka Riti synshar Ri ne Constitution jong ka ri India lem bad ia kiwei pat ki hok ha ka synshar paidbah na ka bynta ki nongshong shnong jong ka ri.
U President HITO u la ong ba ka jingpynmih ia kane ka hukum ka long ka bym don nongrim bad ka bym shongnia satia namar ki paidbah ki don ia ka hok ban jied ia ki nongmihkhmat bad ruh ban ialehkmen na ka bynta ki kyrtong jong ki kiba ioh ia ka jingjop, kata la kilong na kino kino ki party sain pyrthei.
“Ka rukom pynpaw jong kane ka hukum ban khang ia kino kino ki jingiaid rally bad kiwei pat ha baroh kawei ka district khlem ki daw bad ki nongrim kiba biang ka long kaba sngew bynniaw shibun.
Nalor kata la pyntreikam ia kane ka hukum khlem da bishar bniah kan ktah khlem nongrim ia ki paidbah babun balang," u la bynrap.
Nalor kata u Bah Donbok u la kdew ruh ba ka jinglong jingman kumba ka long mynta kim don satia kino kino ki jingjia jong ka jingiakynad bad ka jingkdew halor kiba kum kine ki jingjia ka long ka bym don nongrim, hynrei lyngba kane ka jingpynmih hukum baroh ki nongshong shnong hapoh East Khasi Hills ki la shah pynduh noh ia ki hok bad ka jinglaitluid ka jong ki ban pynpaw, ha ka liang ka leit ka wan bad ban pynlong ia ka jingialum paidbah, jingialang, rally bad kiwei pat da ka lynti jong ka jingjaijai, kata katba ia ki jingiakhih ba jai jai, ki proseshon bad kiwei pat la ju pynlong khlem kano kano ka jingpynkhein kyndon ha baroh ki bynta jong ka nongbah.
“Kumta ruh haba pynshong nongrim halor kitei ki jingshisha baroh, ka Seng ka kyrpad jur ia phi ba phin weng noh ia katei ka hukum ba la pynmih ha ka 23 tarik Jymmang khnang ba ki hok jong ki paidbah nongshong shnong kin ym shah iuhroit bad shah ktah," ong shuh shuh utei u nongialam ha ka dorkhas.

“Shen ngin lah ban pyndep ia kane ka kam. Mynta ka dang sah ban pynlong sa ia ka public hearing," ong u Myntri.

Ka jingtohkit halor kane ka la iaid shakhmat bad la register UD case katkum ka case Umiam PS UD Case No 14/2024 dated 26.05.24.
Ka Seng Hynniewtrep Youth Council (HYC) ka la aiti ia ka memorandum sha ka Director General of Police (DGP) ka Meghalaya ka Kong Idashisha Nongrang ha kaba ka la kyntu ba kan tuklar lem ha kaba iadei bad ka jingeh namar ka jingjyllei jong u drok hapoh ka Jylla.
Ha kane ka jingleit iakynduh ia ka DGP ka Jylla ha ka 27 tarik mynta u bnai, u President ka HYC u Bah Roy Kupar Synrem u la ong ba ka tnat pulit ka dei ban pynkhlain shuh shuh ia ki rukom treikam khnang ban lah ban tehlakam ia ka jingwan rung jong u drok shapoh ka Jylla.
“Ngi aijingmut ba ka tnat pulit ka dei ban shim da ki sienjam kiba tyngeh ban tehlakam ia ka jingwan rung jong u drok shapoh ka Jylla.
Ngi aijingmut ruh ia ka tnat pulit ka Jylla, ki shipai Border Security Force kumjuh ia ka tnat Custom & Central Excise ba kin pynlong khah khah ia ki jingtalasi bad ruh ban iatreilang ha ka jingiakhun pyrshah ia ka jingjyllei jong u drok ha ka jylla, kumjuh ban ai ka jingiatreilang bad ki bor shnong bad ban talasi khah khah ha ki jaka rung jaka mih sha ka Jylla," ong u president ka HYC.
Nalor kata u la ong ruh ba ka NDPS Act, 1985 ka la don lypa ia ki kyndon ba pyrkhing pyrshah ia ki kam khaii bad dih drok.
Watla ki kam khaii drok ki dei ki bym lah ban lait jamin katkum ka Act, hynrei la iohi ha kiba bun ki khep ba ki nongkhaii drok ki ioh lait noh na ka jingshah set namar kiba bun ki sienjam ki bym biang.
Ki don bun ki case jong ki briew bala pynngat ha ka NDPS hynrei ia kiba la hap pynkut noh namar ka jingbym treikam lane ka jingbym iahap ki kyndon.
“Ka jinglait shah pynsaja jong ki nongleh kam bymman hapoh ki case NDPS ka buh jingma shibun ia ka imlang ka sahlang bad ka pynduh mynsiem ruh ia ki paidbah ha kaba iadei bad ki rukom treikam jong ka ain.
Kumta ka long kaba donkam ia ki Investigating Agencies/Prosecutors ba ki dei ban khmih bad pyntreikam bha ia ki kyndon ain kiba la don khnang ban poi sha ka thong kumba la angnud katkum ka ain," ong u Bah Synrem.
“Kumta ruh ban poi sha ka thong kaba katkum ka Act bad ban pynthikna ia ka rai pynrem jong ki briew kiba shah pynngat ha ki case NDPS, ki Enforcement agency ka Jylla ki dei ban tip bniah ia ki kyndon jong ka Act ha ka por ba pynlong ia ka jingtohkit khnang ba ka jingtian bishar kan long kaba iaid beit iaid ryntih.
Haba pynpaw halor ka jingdonkam ban pynsngewthuh ha kaba iadei bad ki kyndon halor ka jingioh pdiang ia ki mar tuh, u president ka HYC u la ong, “Ka Section 317 jong ka  Bharatiya Nyaya Sanhita, 2023 (Repealing the Indian Penal Code, 1860), ka ban sdang treikam naduh ka 1 tarik Naitung 2024 ka don ia ki kyndon pyrshah ia kino kino kiba thied ia ki mar tuh.
U la ong ruh ba lyngba ki nongdih drok bad kiba haiing hasem jong ki, ki la ioh jingtip ruh halor ki jingjia ha kaba ki nongdih drok tang ban ioh pisa ban thied drok kim banse ban tuh na la ki jong ki iing ki sem da kaba die tad dor ia ki tiar ki tar.
“Kumta khnang ban pynshai paidbah ha kaba iadei bad kane ka kyndon ain ka Tnat ka dei ban ialap bad pynshai paidbah khnang ba ki paidbah kin sngewbha ba ka long beain ban thied ia ki mar tuh ba wan die da ki briew kiba kyrni ha ki jingdih drok," ong shuhshuh u nongialam ka Seng.

Ka team kaba khlieh dor heh kan wan nyngkong bud kiwei pat katkum ka buh dor ba ki thied.
Lah ban ioh iaki form naduh 1 tarik haduh 6 tarik Jylliew 2024 haka dor T.200.
Kiba thied kidei ban suhlang bad ka receipts haka tender form.

Ka Central Integrated Pest Management Centre (CIPMC), kaba hap haka Ministry of Agriculture & Farmers Welfare, Directorate Plant Protection, Quarantine & Storage kala pynlong iaka jingai jinghikai kaba ar sngi iaki nongrep ha rilum Jaintia ban iada ia u jyntang bad u soh kba haki lyngkha ha Jowai.
Kane ka jingai jinghikai kala sdang haka sngi Palei bad kut haka sngi Thohdieng.
Ha kane ka jingai jinghikai nalor ba pyni ha pyrda la ialam ruh sha ki lyngkha iaki nongrep kiba don haduh 40 ngut kumno ban iada ia u jyntang bad u kba ha ki lyngba na ki khniang kiba wan hiar thma ia u jingthung kaba wanrah ka jingduh nong kaba khraw iaki paid nongrep.
Ia kane ka jingai jinghikai la pynlong ha jaka ai jinghikai ka ophis u District Agriculture Officer, West Jaintia Hills District.
Kane ka training la tip kum ka “HRD-Orientation Training Programme for Farmer on Integrated Pest Management in Paddy Cultivation".
Ha kane ka jingai jinghikai la iadonlang u District Agriculture Officer, EMH nalor ki riewshemphang Central Integrated Pest Management Centre (CIPMC), Shillong kiba kynthup ia Plant Protection Officer (PPO), Gokulraam M, u Dr. Devaraja KP (APPO), ka kong Aroti Hazaeika (APPO).
Ia ka jingialang la pyniaid da u ma S Syngkon Agriculture Development Officer.
Ka thong jong kane ka training ka dei ba ki nongrep kin ioh jinghikai, ban tip ia ka Integrated Pest Management (IPM) kila lad ban iada na ki khiang kiba pynjulor bad kiba iarap pynheh pynsan iaki jingthung ne u kba ha pyntha kba.
Kine ki khniang kiba pynsniew iaki jingthung ki dei kiba la tip kum Yellow Stem Borer, Leaf Folder, Gundi Bug, Rice Blast, Rice Leaf Spot & Udbatta Disease.
Baroh kine ki khniang ki dei kiba pynsniew ia u jyntang kba bad u soh kba da kaba sam thliew iaki sla, kiba pynsong iaki sla, pynsiew iaki symboh bad kiwei kiwei.
Ha ka jingkren plie ia kane ka training, U District Agriculture Officer, EMH Passah u la kyntu ia ki nongrep ban pyndonkam hok iaki jinghikai kaba kila ioh na kane ka jingai jinghikai ka CIPMC khnang ban myntoi haka rep ka riang.
Ha kane ka sngi la pynlong ruh ia ka jingleit jurip sha ki pynthor ki hali, ha ki them jong ka Wah Myntdu ha Syntu Ksiar ban shim jingkhein kaba la tip kum ka Agro Ecosystem Analysis ha kaba la phiah ia ki nongrep ha ki 4 kynhun na ka bynta ka leh ia ka jingjurip ia ki jait khiang ki ba pynjulor bad ki khiang kiba ai jingiada ia u kba.
Haba kren bad u Plant Protection Officer (PPO), Gokulraam M, u la ong ba la leh iakane ka jingjurip da ki nongrep kan long ba ki nongrep kin lah ban shim ia kano kano ka rai ha kaba ia dei kumno ban iada ia u kba ha pynthor hali kat kum ka jinglong ka suin bneng, ka jaka ne kyndew, ka jinglong jingman jong ka um bad ki jait khniang.
Ki nongrep dalade hi ki hap ban leh ia kane sha pynthor khnang ban tip bad ban shim jingkhein bad pynkreh ia ki jingthoh kaba ki shem ha ka jingrip jong ki.

Ka  Lyngkhuh snem thymmai Khasi la rakhe ha ka por miet jong ka 4 bad 5 tarik Naiwieng, 2021 ha ïing jong I Bah Spiton Kharakor ha Nongkseh.
Ha ka miet shiteng synñia baroh ki ba la don lang ha kata ka sngi rakhe, ki la ïa shim bynta ban tbeh jingshai ïa u snem thymmai ba la lam khmat da I Bah Spiton Kharakor, Bah Herman Nongrum bad Bah Raphael Warjri, khliehduh jong ka synjuk ki barikor Khasi- Riti Academy of Visual Arts, Shillong.
Ha kane ka jingrakhe I Bah Spiton Kharakor I la batai bniah ia ka jingshem jongi ha ka ba tih sani bad pynurlong ka jingthmu kum ban ainguh ainam ia u paralok jongi u ba la khlad noh, I Bah B Nishan Wahlang (Bam kwai ha dwar U Blei).
Ka la jia ha ka 23 tarik Naiwieng, 2018 ha ba I Bah Herman Nongrum I la pur khana ha kata ka sngi lyngkhuh snem iap ba-ar jong I Bah B Nishan Wahlang ha ka shlem treikam jong ka Riti Academy, ha ka ba la don lang ki rangbah kum u Bah HS Shylla (Bam kwai ha dwar U Blei) bad I Bah Bindo M Lanong ryngkat kiwei kiwei ki rangbah bad longkmie na ka kur Wahlang bad kur Warjri.
Mar ïa dap shiteng synñia la pynkhreh ban thang da ki dongmusa kum ka dak ban pdiang ia u snem thymmai.
Ka long kaei kaei ka ba sngewphieng ban shahshkor na ki kyntien jong I Bah Herman Nongrum ha ba la kren mardor ïa ka khana halor ka tipbriew tipblei jong ki paidbynriew Khasi ba la kyrpad ban thoh, ha ka ba la bynshet kylliang pat ban thwet ïa ka snem thymmai jong ki paidbynriew Khasi.
Ka jingïakren ka long ka ba byllai, ba kynsai bad ba jylliew, hynrei ka ba kongsan tam ka long ba I Bah Herman bad I Bah Nishan Wahlang ki la kular ba dei ban smai man la ka khep ba rakhe snem thymmai na ka bynta ban long tipbriew tipblei.
Kata ka jingkren ka la shon ha dohnud jong ki ba la ïa don lang ha kata ka sngi khamtam kum ha kane ka juk ba la hiardor ka akor longbriew manbriew.
Kumta ka snem thymmai Khasi kan long ka jingkyrsiew ia ka imlang sahlang ban long ki ba tipbriew tipblei barabor ha la ka jingim ha ka imlang sahlang.
Ka kynto ka la don naduh ki snem ba la leit la iathuh u Bah Raphael Warjri ha ba u Bah AB Hynñiewta u la thoh kawei ka kot halor ka rukom kheiñ sngi kheiñ ïa ki Khasi katkum u bnai bneng.
Katkum kata ka kot ki longshwa manshwa Khasi ki kheiñ khatlai bnai shi snem, arphew phra sngi shibnai bad phra sngi shi taïew.
Ka jingshem jong I Bah Spiton Kharakor ruh ka byrshem hangta bad la nang tih nang thwet shuh shuh haduh ban da urlong ka jingthmu ban pynmih ka almanak Khasi ba khatlai bnai shisnem ka ba la pyrshang ban pynphuh pynphieng man la ka lyngkhuh snem ba rakhe ia ka sngi mih bnai nyngkong jong u snem thymmai.
Ha ka imlang sahlang la kham jwat ban iaidlait na ka almanak na shiliang duriaw (Gregorian Calendar) ka ba la pdiang salonsar ha satlak pyrthei kynthup ha Ri Khasi.
Hynrei ka long ka ba donkam ban pynneh ïa ki snap jong ka riti tynrai Khasi, bad la duriap bad buddien ïa kata ka kam bah jong ka jaitbynriew da ka Riti Academy.
Ha ka jingïakren ha kata ka rakhe sngi lyngkhuh snem la shim ka rai ban thaw da kawei ka lyngwiar kyrpang ban pyrkhat sani halor kane ka jingrakhe man la u snem.

SHILLONG: U Executive Member badei khmih iaka tnad enforcement ka Khasi Hills Autonomous District Council (KHADC) u Bah Teibor Pathaw u la kren shai ba ki sengbhalang kim don bor ban khynra ia ki dukan haba iadei bad ki kot ki sla ba dei ban ioh na ka council, kum ka trading lane labour licence namar kane ka dei ka kamram ka council.
“Ngi la iohi ia kane ka jingleit khynra kine ki sengbhalang ia ki dukan haba iadei bad ka jingdon ne em ki kot ki sla ba biang ba ioh na district council, hynrei kim don bor ban leh ia kane hynrei dei tang ka tnad enforcement wing jong ka district council kaba lah ban leh ia kane ka kam lada I donkam," la ong u Bah Pathaw.
U la ong ruh ba lada kine ki snengbhalang ki lap ba ka don ka jingkhaii beain bad ba ki don ki briew ba pyniaid ia ki dukan lane ki kam jong ki khlem pat da ioh ia ka trading licence na ka district council ki dei ban pyntip shuwa sha ka tnad ba dei khmih ia kane ka mat bad kumta naka liang ka tnad kan sa shimkhia ban phah ia ki enforcement ban khmih bniah ia ki kot ki sla jong kino kino ki dukan.
Ula iathuh ba ki don ki sengbhalang kiba ju pyntip sha ka district council haba don ki briew kiba trei khlem da ioh iaka labour licence naka district council bad kumta naka tnad la shimkhia bad la phah leit sha kito ki jaka ban leit phah peit bad ki don ruh ki sengbhalang ki bym pyntip iaka council.
La kyntu ruh ia ki sengbhalang ba lada ki lap ba don ba leh beain ne iaid lait iaka district council haba iadei bad ka trading lane ka labour licence kidei ban pyntip shuwa sha ki tnad badei khmih ia kane ka kam ha KHADC.
U Bah Pathaw u la pynpaw ruh ia ka jing sngewkhia haba iadei bad ka rukom long rukom man ka tnad enforcement namar kumba long mynta ki dang duna palat ki kki nongtrei haka tnad enforcement ka KHADC.
“Ka kamram ka tnad ka long ban phah ia ki enforcement ban leit ban jurip haba iadei bad ki kot ki sla jong ki dukan lada ki la ioh ne em ia ka trading licence naka district council namar ban seng kam neh buh dukan khlem ka jingbit ka council ka long beain bad kumta ka council khnang ban dang lah ban trei kham bha la donkam ban pynbha shuh shuh iaka tnad," u la ong.
U la pynpaw ruh ba kumba long mynta ka KHADC ka dong tang kumba 76 ngut ki pulit enforcement wing ha district council bad kumta la don ka jingthmu ban kham pynbha iaka rukom treikam ka tnad ha council.
U la iathuh ruh baka la ju don ruh ka jingiakren bad ka sorkar jylla ban kham pynkhlain iaka tnad enforcement wing lyngba ka grant-in-aid sha kaka district council, hynrei naduh u snem 2014 ka council ka khlem ioh pisa shuh naka sorkar jylla haba iadei ban pynkhlain ia kane ka tnad.
“Haba iadei bad kane ngi la dep iakren bad u EM badei khmih iaka tnad Trade u Bah Paul Lyngdoh bad u Deputy CEM u Bah Pyniaid Sing Syiem ba ngin pynkhlain ia kane ka tnad enforcement wing khnang ba ngin lah ban pyntreikam naka bynta ban peit lane khynra haba iadei bad ki kam beain ba iadei bad ka trade lane labour licence," u la ong.

Ha katei ka jingjurip jong ka MSPCB kaba la wan u Assistant Environment Engineer  MSPCB, u Bah S Syiem, ki dkhot ka SEPSD haka jingialam u Joint Secretary SEPSD u samla Diamond Dhar, ryngkat ki waheh shnong ka Khliehmyntriang u Ma J Dkhar, u Ma H. Phawa Waheh Shnong Jalyiah bad kiwei.
Naka liang ka MSPCB kala ong ba hap ban leh ïaka test, khnang ban lap laka lyer ne haw ka shah ktah na ka tdem ba mih na ka kharkhana.
Kane ka kharkhana ka pynmih ruh ïaka jingsma iwtung na ki jaboh ba mih na kane ka kharkhana, kaba la kynnoh ba ka ktah ia ka koit ka khiah jong ki nongshnong shnong, ki nongleit nongwan bad ia ki khynnah jong kawei ka skul kaba don hajan kane ka kharkhana.

La kyntu ia u myntri ka koit ka khaih ban shimkhia ia kane ka kam, na ka bynta ban pynkynriah ia kane ka kharkhana sha kawei pat ka jaka ba iadei bad ki kharkhana  kaba jngai naki shnong ki thaw.

JOWAI: Ka HK Singh Memorial Lower Primary School kala rakhe ïaka jingdap 50 snem ka jingiaid lynti jong ka naduh bala seng ha u snem 1968.
Ïa kane ka jingrakhe dap 50 snem kane ka skul la wan ban plie paidbah da u Ma Lahkmen Rymbui, Myntri ka Pule Puthi ka Jylla haka sngi Saitjaiñ.
Nalor u Myntri ka tnad pule puthi la ïadonlang u Rev. Derrick Pariat, President UUNEI uba long kum u symbud kongsan haryngkat ki khynnah skul bad ki nonghikai kiba barim bad kiba mynta.
U Ma Rupaia Lamarr Chairman SMC, ula ïathuh ïaka history lyngkot ka skul.
Ula ïathuh ba ka Ka Balang Jowai ka dei ka Balang Unitarian kaba nyngkong ha kine ki thain kaba kynthup ia ka Assam bad ka Meghalaya bad la seng nyngkong haka 18 tarik u September 1887.
Dei hadien ba la seng ïaka Balang U Babu Hajom Kissor Singh ula iohi ïaka jingdonkam ban seng ïaka skul ban pyllait ïa ki nongshong shnong na ka jingsah dum namar ka jingbym nang ban pule bad thoh tar.
Ha u snem 1893 ula sdang iaka Unitarian Free School, hynrei hadien ba ula mih na Jowai kane ka skul kala jah noh ha u snem 1904.
Hynrei ka balang kala shimkhia ban seng biang iaka skul ha u 1968 bad la pynsah nam haka kyreng u Babu HK Singh bad ki nonghikai ba nyngkong ki kynthup ïaka Kong Wanlang Laloo, ka Kong H. Shylla bad ka Kong E. Pakma.
U Ma Lahkmen haba kren kum u kongsan ula ai ka jingiaroh ïaki nongialam ka balang kiba ïohi jngai iaka jingkongsan ka pule ka puthi, kumjuh ia kiba mynta kiba la tynrong ka jingkitkhlieh ban pyntyllun ïaka shalyntem kane shlem ka ai jinghikai.
Ula ong ba sorkar na ka por sha ka por ka pynkylla iaka syllabus bad bud ruh iaka rukom pyniaid ka NCERT ban pynjanai iaka jingsam jingnang jingtad sha ki khynnah katkum ka juk mynta.
“Ka sorkar kala dep phah pyntbit palat 3500 ngut ki nonghikai bad wat hapdeng ka jinghiran pisa ka sorkart kala ai jingiarap iaki spah tylli skul ban pynbiang iaka jingdonkam jong ki ban pynbha iaka pule puthi haka jylla,"la ong u Myntri Pule Puthi.
Ha kane ka jingplie iaka lyngkhuh snem kane ka skul, kaba yn rakhe baroh shi snem lynter la ioh ruh ka jingkren na u Ma T Passah Headmaster HK Singh Memorial Secondary School, u Ma Mehun Sutong khynnah skul barim, u Ma D. Pohchen bad la pynphuh pynphieng ia kane ka sngi da ki jingrwai bad ki jingshad na ki khynnah katei ka skul bad ka jingot ïa u cake da ki lai ngut ki nonghikai barim.

JOWAI: Ka jingthmu jong ki Pulit Assam ban shna ktem pulit ha Khatkasla ka jaka kaba hap ha Khappud Meghalaya-Assam kala pulom noh hadien ka jingpyni bor ki ar district haka jingiadonlang ki pulit bad u paidbah ka shnong Khatkasla bad Psiar haka sngi Palei.
U Border Magistrate ka West Jaiñtia Hills u Bah Ferdinand Basan, u Dy. SP West Jaiñtia Hills u Bah Donkupar Moksha kila hiar shuwa haka sngi Balang pynsangeh ïaka jingthmu shna ktem ki Pulit Assam ha katei ka jaka, hynrei u Pulit bad ka bor synshar ka Assam kila leh bymsuidniew.
Kane ka jaka ba thmu ki pulit Assam ki shna ktem pulit ka dei ha Iurim Biam, kaba hap ha Khatkasla ka lynti ban leit sha Umkhyrmi bad Mokoilum ba hap ha West Karbi Anglong, Assam.
Kane ka jaka ka jngai tang kumba 10-15 KM na Mokoilum.
Hadien ba ki Pulit Assam kila leh bymsuidniew ïaka jingbthah jong u Border Magistrate ka West Jaiñtia Hills, hynne ka sngi Palei kila hiar biang sha katei ka jaka ryngkat ka kynhun Pulit, u paidbah nongshong shnong da ki spah spah ngut bad hadien ka jingïakren ki pulit ka Assam kila hap ban phet na katei ka jaka bad pynpra iaka ktem jong ki bad kit ïaki tum ki tam jong ki.
Haka sngi Balang ka bor synshar jong ka West Karbi Anglong kila wan sha katei ka jaka haka jingialam u Border Magistrate, West Karbi Anglong, Assam ryngkat ka pyrton pulit bad CRP.
U Border Magistrate jong ka West Jaiñtia Hills U Bah Ferdinand Basan ula ïasaid bad ieng pyrshah tyngeh ïaka jingthmu jong ka Assam ban shna ktem pulit ha katei ka jaka.
Ula dawa na ki bor synshar district ka West karbi Anglong, Assam ban pyni da ki kot ki sla, halor ka jingkam jong ki ba ka dei ka sorkar Assam kaba bthah ïaki ban shna ïaka ktem shipai.
Kane ka jaka ka dei kaba kila dep ban lur da ka puh shilum bad khyllem ïaki dieng bad kila dep ruh ban shna ïa iing trep ban shna ïaka ktem Pulit jong ka Assam.
La bun bun sien ki Pulit jong ka Assam kila thmu ban shna ktem pulit hakatei ka jaka, hynrei mynta ka kynti ka sur u paidbah kala jop.
Kumban shu pynkynmaw Kyllalyngkot 29, 2018 ruh ha kane ka juh ka shnong ka Assam kala wan da ki puh shilum ban pynkhyllem bun tylli dieng bad pynmadan ïaka jaka ban shna Out Post hi, hynrei ka bor District jong ka West Jaiñtia Hills kala hiar ban pyn sangeh mardor ka jingshna ne jingtih lum jong ka sorkar Assam Hadien ba u Pulit Assam ula dep pynpra ïaka ktem, la lum jingialang ha iing Waheh Shnong Psiar haka jingiadonlang u Waheh Shnong Khatkasla bad Moolaber, u MLA Nujorki Sungoh, MDC, Dolloi Elaka Raliang, Rikut Parien nongialam barim ka JSU bad kiwei kiwei.
La rai ha kane ka jingialang ban ïakynduh ïa u Myntri Rangbah, Myntri kam Pohiing ka Jylla bad ban dawa mardor ban buh iaka ktem pulit jong ka sorkar Meghalaya ha kitei ki shnong.
Halor kane ka jingjia u Myntri Rangbah ka Jylla Conrad K Sangma ula shimkhia ban iakren bad ka sorkar Assam bad mar mar U Myntri Rangbah ka Assam Sarbananda Sonowal ula bthah ïaki Assam police bad mih na katei ka jaka, la ong u Myntri kam Pohiing ka Jylla u James K Sangma.

Lah ban pynkynmaw ba ka KSU kala ïasnohktilang bad NBAJAC naduh ba sdang jong ka jingdawa ban pynkynriah ia ka ophis C&RD Block na Wapung sha Narpuh bad ban buh iaka kane ka ophis ha ka shnong Lumshnong.
Ka KSU ka iadon bynta ruh bad katei ka Committee ha ka jingleit ia kynduh ia u Myntri Rangbah ka jylla u Conrad K Sangma ha ka tarik 13/09/2018 bad la buh ruh ia ka jingdawa ban pynneh ia ka C&RD ha Lumshnong.

U Myntri Rangbah ha kato ka por, u ong ba u dangshu shimti thymmai ia ka shuki Myntri Rangbah, um da shai bha ha ka jingiadei bad kane ka kam bad ula kyntu ban ailad ba un pyrkhat shwa katto katne por da kaba kular ruh ban shimkhia ban bishar bniah ia kane ka jingdawa.

Ka thaiń Narpuh ka la donkam kyrkieh ia kane ka ophis badon kam tam namar ngi la roi ha ka jingbun briew, bad u pud u sam ba iar bad katkum ki jingdawa ka por ka Narpuh kam dei ban shu sah beit hajuh khlem kino kino ki lad jingpynroi na ka sorkar bad ka donkam ia ki jingkylla la ha ka liang ka roi ka par bad ha ka ioh ka kot, la ong u Deibormi Dkhar General Secretary KSU Narpuh Circle.

Ïa kane ula ong haka jingialang pyniasoh jong u ryngkat bad ki dkhot bad nongialam ka AJSU na Shangpung Unit, Nartiang Circle, Jowai Circle, Mudop Unit kiba la pynïasoh ïalade sha ka JSM haka sngi Saitjain haka jingialang kaba long ha ïingdorbar ka shnong Khliehmyntriang, East Jaiñtia Hills District.
“Ki Seng bhalang kila nang nang bun ha rilum Jaiñtia, pynban ka jaidbynriew kala nang nang shah ktah haka jinglong jingman tynrai jong ngi bad ka jingma ka ap lada ngim ia tylli ban ieng kawei ban iada iaka jaidbynriew,", la ong u Pillar bad bynrap ba haka jingiohi jong u ka jaidbynriew jong ngi kam slem shuh ban shah tyllep ha ki nongwei la haka khaii ka pateng, ka kolshor, ka riti ka dustur bad ula ong ba ka daw ba u rung ban pyniasoh sha ka JSM ka don ki nongialam kiba don ka mynsiem rangbah kiba sngewthuh ban kit ban bah na ka bynta ka iap ka im ka jaidbynriew.

Ha kane ka sngi la ïoh ruh ka jingkren na U General secretary JSM u Ma Edie Lamare, na U Ardipaul Rymbai Chairman ka JSM Social Cell , na U Shnalad Rymbai President JSM eastern region bad kiwei kiwei.
SHILLONG: Ha ka sien ba nyngkong hadien ka jingwad bniah ka jingiakhih, ka jinglum kot kaba la arphew snem bad hadien ka jingiakynduh saw sien ka Advisory Committee, On Legislation and Legal Issues, ka la shim ia ka rai ban khot ia u Bah John F Kharshiing, Spokesperson, Federation of Khasi States, & Chairman, Ka Dobar Ki Khlieh Nongsynshar Ka Ri Hynniewtrep, hakhmat ki longheh KHADC ha ka 4 tarik June 2019, ha Conference Hall, KHADC, ban ai jingpynshai halor ka Instrument of Accession and Annexed Agreement 17 August 1948, ha ka jingialang kaba la pyniaid da u Bah Pynshngainlang N Syiem, MDC, Chairman, KHADC, ha ka jingiadonlang i Bah Teinwell Dkhar, MDC, Chief Executive Member, KHADC, Bah Pyniaid Sing Syiem, MDC, Deputy Chief Executive Member, KHADC, Bah Titosswell Chyne, MDC, Executive Member, Bah Martle N Mukhim, MDC, Executive Member, Bah Lambor Malngaiang, MLA & MDC, Chairman, Advisory Committee, Administration and Financial Reforms, Bah Sherbolang Mawlong, MDC, Chairman, Committee Youth Affairs, Bah M Kharkrang, Secretary, Legislative, Bah Lamphrang Blah, MDC, Leader Opposition, Kong Grace Mary Kharpuri, MDC, Shri. Ronnie V Lyngdoh, MDC, Bah Fantin Joseph Lakadong, MDC, Bah Gabrial Wahlang, MDC, Bah Bajop Pyngrope, MDC, Bah Carness Sohshang, MDC, KHADC, u Bah R. Kharjarin, Pleadar KHADC, Dr S Lamare, bad Dr B. L. Nongbri, ki dkhot (Member), Advisory Committee, On Legislation and Legal Issues bad kiwei ki officer KHADC.
Ha katei ka jingialang, ha kaba plie ia ka jingialang u Bah PN Syiem, Chairman, KHADC, u la pynsngew ba ka por ka dawa ban wad ki lynti ban thaw ki lad ki lynti kumno ban ioh jingshai bad jingiada halor ki hok jong ka jaidbynriew bad ha kaba u la pynsngew ba kawei na ki lynti ka long ban bishar bniah halor ki dulir iateh bad ki dulir kular (Instrument of Accession and Annexed Agreement) kaba la soi bad mynjur ka Sorkar India bad ka Federation of Khasi States, ha ka 15 December 1947 bad 17 August 1948 ha shuwa ka 26 January 1950 ba la pynjari ia ka Constitution Ri India bad ban bishar lada kane ka dulir ka dang im ne ka la iap khnang ban sngewthuh kumno kan iada ia ngi nalor ki kyndon Sixth Schedule.
Ha katei ka jingialang na ka liang u Bah John F Kharshiing, u la pynlait ha ka sien kaba nyngkong ia ka shithi jong u Sir Akbar Hydari, Governor Assam sha u Shri. Jawaharlal Nehru, kaba kren shapang ka dulir IOA & AA kaba long ruh kum ka Standstill Agreement kaba la ia mynjur bad ki Hima Khasi States – Ka Federation of Khasi States, ha ka 16 July 1947 kaba kren shai ba kan neh tang AR SNEM, bad u la pyni ruh ia ka IOA & AA kaba 9 tarik August 1947 bad ka IOA & AA kaba 17 August 1948 kaba la mynjur da ka Sorkar India hynrei kaba la weng noh ia ki kyntien AR SNEM.
Wat hadien ba la ia soi ia kitei ki dulir hapdeng ki jingshah byrngem ki Khlieh Nongsynshar ki la lah ban ksoh ia ki kyndon lyngba ka Annexed Agreement, hynrei ha ka juh ka por u la pynshai ba ka jaidbynriew khasi ha ki snem 1947 ka la kad ar liang kawei kaba la lam khmat ki Khlieh Nongsynshar bad ha kawei ka liang kaba ialam da u Rev JJM Nichols Roy, uba la dei ruh ha ka jingshisha u Secretary uba nyngkong jong ka Federation of Khasi States.
Kumno la leit mih ka jingiapher jingmut ym nang sngewthuh hynrei kumba ka paw u Bah JJM Nichols Roy u la pyrshah namar la mih ka jingong ba dei tang ki 25 Hima Khasi States, kiba la soi ia ka IOA & AA katba ki British Sirdarship kiba rit kiba tang shi shnong, lane lai Shnong, kumba 29 tylli bad ki 19 Elaka Jaintia Hills kim shym ioh ka kyrdan IOA & AA, bad ka jingthmu jong u Rev JJM Nichols Roy ka la long ban ioh ia ka jingsynshar kaban pyntylli ia baroh ki jaka kynthup ki Hima Khasi States, ki British Sirdarship bad ka Jaintia Hills.
Ha ka juh ka por u la long u nongmihkhmat uba la ioh leit mih khmat sha ka Constituent Assembly bad u la long uba jan ia u Premier Assam u Gopinath Bordoloi, Kumta wat lada ia katei ka dulir la dep mynjur da ka Sorkar India, hynrei namar ki jingsuh buit ka Assam kim shym ailad ia katei ka dulir bad ki la pynrung jubor ia ki 25 Hima Khasi States hapoh ka Sixth Schedule hapoh ka jingsynshar ka Assam.
U Rev JJM Nichols Roy, u la pynpaw ia ka jingbabe ba ka jingkthang ia katei ka jingleh donbor ka Sorkar Assam ha kaba u la pynpaw ba ki la pynkylla ia ka draft bad ka jingai jingmut ka Sub-Committee, Drafting Committee, Constituent Assembly, ha kaba u Bah JJM Nichols Roy u la pynpaw ia ka jingbitar ba ki rangbah nongialam Assam ki la bsuh kyndon ba ka Sixth Schedule kan long hapoh ka jingkhmih ka jylla Sorkar Assam ym kumba mut u Rev JJM Nichols Roy, ba ka Sixth Schedule kan don ka jingiadei kaba kyrpang bad ka Sorkar India kumba la kdew ha ka IOA & AA.
U Rev JJM Nichols Roy, u la ong ha ki jingthoh jong u ba namar u la shah shet bad u la kylla long tang marwei kum u riewlum um shym don lad bad leh da kumwei bad ban shu pdiang beit ia kaei kaba la pynkylla ka Sorkar Assam.
Katba ha kawei ka liang u Sayeed Mohammed Sadulla, u Premiere Assam (uba ngi khot Chief Minister hadien ka 1950) ha ka jingkren jong u hapoh Parliament ha ka juh ka por ba pynskhem ia ka draft Sixth Schedule u la ong ba kane ka jingleh donbor ia ki Hima Khasi States kan wanrah jingeh hadien habud ia ka Sorkar India, bad u la kyntu ia ki dkhot ka Constituent Assembly kiban sa bteng hadien ka 1950 ba kin pynbeit bad pyndep ia ki jingiakut ki jingkular katkum ka IOA & AA.
Kumta, u Bah John F Kharshiing, u la kren skhem ba ka IOA & AA ka dang im bad ka Sorkar India kam don lynti lait na kaban pyntreikam ia ki jingiateh ki jingkular baroh ha kaba kan mih ka Sorkar jong ka Federation of Khasi States.
Shuh shuh haba jubap halor ka jingkylli balei bad kaei kaba pynlong ia ki Khlieh Nongsynshar ki Hima Khasi States ban pyrshah ia ka Sixth Schedule, u Bah John F Kharshiing, u la kren shai ba ki Hima Khasi States naduh ki snem 1947-48 ki la pyrshah ia ka Sixth Schedule namar ki nongwei ki lah ban long MDC kumba paw ha ki kyndon Sixth Schedule haduh kine ki sngi, u la pynkynmaw ba ha u snem 1952 u lat u la thung saw ngut kiba shuh sieh da ki MDC nongwei kaba la wanrah ka jingiakhih kaba jur hapoh Shillong, bad nangta ha u snem 1972 ar ngut ki MDC nongwei ki la jop na Laban bad na Laitumkhah kum ki MDC, katba da ka nongrim ka IOA & AA tang ki Khasi kin ioh long dkhot kane ka dei ka jingiapher ka jingpyrshah kaba hakhmat eh.
Shuh shuh u la ong ba katkum ka IOA & AA ka jylla Khasi States ka la dei ban paw naduh ba sdang ha ka Constitution Ri India kum ka jylla kaba kyrpang, hynrei u la ong ka sakhi jong ka jingim ki dulir IOA & AA ka kyntien “Khasi States: ki sah kut hapoh ka First Schedule hapoh u pud ka jylla Assam haduh kine ki sngi, bad u la kyntu jur ia ki MDC ba kin pyrkhat sani bha ia kane ka bynta ha kaba u long uba kloi ban pynshai shuh shuh halor katei ka phang.
U Bah John F Kharshiing, u la pynsngew ba kan jinglada iarap ban iada ia ka Ri lada ki kyntien Dorbar Kur, Dorbar Shnong, Dorbar Raid bad Dorbar Hima, ki paw shai kumjuh ruh kan jinglada long ka jingiada lada ki kyntien Syiem, Lyngdoh, Sirdar, Myntri, Basan, Syiem Raid, Lyngdoh Raid, Sordar Raid, Dolloi, Rangbah Shnong, Sordar Shnong, Myntri Shnong, Rangbah Kur ki paw shai hapoh ka Constitution Ri India kumba paw shai ki Gram Panchayat, District Panchayat (shnong nongwei) hapoh Constitution Ri India lyngba ka Article 243.

Da U Soolangki D. Laloo K a 5 tarik u Jylliew kaba ngi tip kum ka World Environment Day ka dei ka sngi ha kaba ki ri ha shityllup ka pyrthei ha ka thong ban pynneh pynsah ia ka jingitynnad ka mei mariang bad ki sawdong sawkun jong ka, ki la shim ka jingkitkhlieh ban leh shibun ki kam kum ha ka ban thung ia thied, ki siej, ki syntiew ki skud bad kiwei kiwei ki rukom leh ba iahap bad ka thong jong ka World Environment Day.
Kum u nongthoh haba phai sha kane ka sngi ka wan ka sur ban phalang ha ka pyrkhat pyrdain jong nga ia u wei u riew ieit mariang uba ngim shym la poi pyrkhat ba da ka jingstad bad jingshemphang jong u ki dieng ha ryngkat ki sla jyrngam baphuh itynnad kin iohlad ban neh, ban san bad pynsuhsieng ia ka jingitynnad ki sawdong sawkun ka mei mariang.
Hooid, une u briew wat la um don shuh hangne ha pyrthei shongbasa hynrei ki dak kti bad ki kam ratbah ba u la leh kin long ki mot ba iaineh iaisah bad ieng sakhi ha khmat ka pyrthei teng la pateng.
Kum u pateng kane ka juk haba bishar bad pynshongdor pynshongnia ia ka jingpynmih pyrthei ka Khnap thangbru (Eco-friendly Crematorium) ba la shem bad pynwandur da u ma Kambell Chullai ka long shisha ka jingkyrkhu ym tang na ka bynta kito ki briew ba pyndonkam ia ka hynrei ka long ruh kyrpang ia ka mei mariang ha kaba ki dieng ba ju pom bad pynkhyllem da ki bun tynrai na ka bynta ban pyndep ia ka niam iap, ha kine ki sngi ba mynta laioh ban sakhi ba kine kiei kiei kim don shuh naduh ba la mih kane ka Eco-Friendly Crematorium u ma Kambell Chullai.
Haba pyrshang ban iakren bad katto katne ki riew rangbah ia ki rukom ioh myntoi jongki lyngba ka jingdon kane ka Eco-Friendly Crematorium hapoh ki shnong ki Raij jongki, ki iathuh ba ha ki por mynshwa haman badon ka jingiap hapoh ka Raij ka shnong na ka bynta ban pyndep ia ka niam iap bad pynkhuid ia ka met ha ka syiemding ki hap ban pom bad pynkhyllem da ki bun tylli ki tynrai diengheh hynrei mynta naduh ba la pynmih pyrthei u ma Kambell ia ka khnap (Eco-friendly crematorium) ba iahap kat kum ka jingiaid jong ka por, ka jingpom ia ki dieng kam don shuh bad ruh na ka bynta ban pyndep ia ka niam iap ne pynkhuid ia ka met ha ka syiending ki lah ban pyndonkam tang da ki katto katne ki diengrit kiba la dep pynkhreh lypa.
Shim jingkhein ia ka jingpom bad thyllem ia ki dieng haman badon ka jingiap ki briew haman ki shnong ki thaw, kat kum ka jingiathuh ki riewrangbah, la ong ba ym duna ia ka saw ne san tylli ki dieng hap ban pom ne thyllem, shu antad lada ha ka shi snem kan don haduh 10 ngut kiba iap ha kawei ka shnong, ki diengheh kin hap ban pom bad thyllem haduh 40 tylli, to pyrkhat lada ha ka shisnem ha kawei kawei ka shnong ka raij kin duh kin dam ki diengheh da ki bun phew bun spah tylli, kumno kan long ka lyer kaba ngi ring ngi pynhiar mynsiem, kumno kan long ka shnong ka thaw jongngi, kumno kin long ki lum ki wah jongngi? Une u dei u Dak Jingkylli uba manga maphi kum ki pateng kane ka juk ngi dei ban pyrkhat bad puson bha.

Haba shim ban pynshongnia shongnongrim ia kane ka jingstad bad jingshemphang u ma Kambell Chullai ban shna bad pynwandur ia ka khnap thangbriew (Eco-Friendly Crematorium), lah ban ong bad pynshisha ba u dei shisha u riew ieit mariang uba ki kam jongu ki kren khamsawa hangi ki pateng wat la um don shuh ryngkat bad ngi hangne ha sla pyrthei.
Ko khun ka Bri u hynniewtrep hynniewskum, hato kum ia une u briew, kaei ka kamram jong ngi, hato ka donkam mo ia nga ia phi ban ngin pynkhraw bad tynrong shuh shuh ia ka nam bad ka kyrteng jong u? Haba phai na ka liang jong ka Forest & Environment Department sngewtynnad ban tip ba ia kane ka jingstad bad jingshemphang u ma Kambell Chullai la pynsaphriang shuh shuh ia ka sha kiwei kiwei de ki jaka ki shnong.
Hynrei kum ka sorkar, kaei pat ka kamram jong ka? Hato kan pynkut noh tang na rmiangshyntur ia ka kyrteng, ka nam bad ki kam u ma Kambell Chullai, hato dei hok mo ia u ma Kambell ha kum kane ka juk ka por ba un ioh ka jingithuh ba kham kyrpang lyngba ka sorkar ne na kiwei kiwei ki kynhun kiba la ioh ban mad ia ka jingkyrkhu lyngba ka Eco-Friendly Crematorium u ma Kambell.

AMLAREM: Ki shipai iada khappud Border Security Force (BSF) jong ka Muktapur BOP kila ïoh kurup haduh 51 tylli ki masi kiba thmu ban shallan beaiñ sha Bangladesh.
U Superintendent of Police West Jaiñtia Hills District U Bah Lakador Syiem ula ong ba ïa kine ki masi, ki shipai kila ïoh kurup haka por ba pahara ïaka khappud India Bangladesh.
Ki shipai kila ai ka jingujor eajahar ha ki Pulit jong ka Muktapur PP bad na kaliang jong ki pulit la kyntu ïaki trai masi ne kino kino kiba don jingtip ïa ki masi shah tuh ban wan mih sha thanad ban pyndep ïaki jingdonkam ka aiñ.
K a jingrakhe ia ka sngi pynneh pynsah mariang kaba la sdang naduh ka 5 tarik u Jylliew 1974 da ka United Nations Environment Programme (UNEP) haduh kine ki sngi ka long ka mat kaba donkam ban sngewthuh  ban pynsaphriang ia ka khubor sha baroh ki nongshong shnong ia ki jingma kiba mih na ka jingpynjot pathar ia ki dieng ki siej ne ki khlaw ki btap kiba pynlong ia ka lyer jaboh ban kharoi , kumjuh ia ka jingkhuid jingsuba ka um dih.
La  seng ia ka  UNEP kaba dei kawei na ki tnat ka United Nations Organization ha ka 5tarik u Jylliew 1972 ha ka Stockholm Conference on Human Environment da ka thong ban wanrah ia ka jingpynsngewthuh sha baroh ki kyndong kynshrot ki Ri ka pyrthei ban pynneh pynsah ia ka mariang bad tehlakam ia ki jingshahktah  ki jingthaw ba don jingim bad  ka jinglong jingman ka suinbneng namar ka jingpynjot pathar ia ka mei mariang.
Man la u snem ha ka 5tarik u Jylliew kylleng sawdong ka pyrthei da ki million, billion bad ki trillion tylli ki tynrai dieng bapher bapher la ju thung da ka jingshim bynta da  ki bor sorkar jong ki Ri , ki sengtreimon sngewbha,  ki khynnah skul, ka imlang sahlang bad kiwei kiwei  da ka thong ban wanrah ia ka jingjyrngam ha ki lum ki wah.
Ka sorkar jylla Meghalaya jong ngi mynta u snem 2019 ka la buh thong ban thung kumba shi million tylli ki tynrai dieng katkum ka jingpynpaw u Myntri Rangbah ka jylla.
Ka dei ka kamram jong ngi iwei pa iwei na ki nongshong shnong ban shimkhia bad pyntikna ba ki symbai ne tynrai dieng ba ngi thung  ha ka sngi rakhe  pynneh pynsah mariang ne ha kiwei ki sngi ki dei ban im , heh bad san  ba ka jingthmu kan long kaba jop bad seisoh.
Ka jingthung ia ki tynrai dieng ba kin heh kin san ka long shisha kaba kongsan khnang ba kin lah ban tan sha ki, ia shibun ka lyer jaboh kaba don ha ka haw haw kaba mih na ki tdem jong ki karkhana, ki kali, ki iing ki sem ,ka jingpluh ki khlaw ki btap bad kiwei kiwei ki bynta kiba pynlong ia ka jingkiew jong ka jingshit bad jingkylla ka suinbneng kiba ktah ia ka jingheh jingsan ki jingthung jingtep, ki mrad ,kumjuh ia ka koit ka khiah u khun bynriew ,ka jingtyrkhong, ka jingum ki lum thah, ka jingkiew  ka um ha ki duriaw, ka jingshlei um bad kiwei kiwei ki jingshah ktah.
Kum shibynta ban pynpaw bad kyntu ia ki nongsynshar jong ngi ha kylleng sawdong ka pyrthei da kaba sdang na la ka jong ka Ri  ka samla kynthei na Ri Sweden ka Greta Thunberg  ha u snem ba lah dep ha ka rta ba dang 15snem ka la sdang ia ka “Fridays for Future" movement  da kaba wer ia ki khynnah skul, kolej bad baroh kiba don jingkitkhlieh ia ka lawei bashngain ban lait na ki jingma ia ka jingpynjot ia ka mariang ban mih shakhmat ban leh eiei ha shuwa ba ka por kan dier.
Ha ka nongbah Shillong jong ngi kum ka jingkyrshan ia katei ka phang ha ka 24 tarik u Jymmang mynta u snem, ki samla pule ki lah iaid paidbah na Don Bosco Square sha State Central Library ha ryngkat ka jingaiti ia ki jingai jingmut sha ka sorkar jylla ban shim ki lad ki lynti halor ki jingshah ktah namar ka jingpynjot pathar ia ka mei mariang.
Ka la dei ka por ba ngin sngewthuh bad don ka jingmlien ba ngin thung bujli bun tylli ki symbai ne tynrai dieng lada ngi pom ia uwei u dieng ne jingmlien ban thung dieng katba lah ei  khnang ba kan nym don jingktah ia ka mariang namar ba ngi hap ban pom ia ki dieng ha ki jingdonkam kiba pher bapher jong ngi man la ka sngi.
U khun bynriew um dei ban shu shim kabu tang ia ka myntoi shimet ha ka khaii pateng hynrei u dei ruh ban pyrkhat ia ka pateng ba mynta bad ki ban sa wan khnang ba kin lait na ki jingshitom kiba bun jait, ba kin biang ka bam ka dih, ban lait na shibun ki jingshah ktah.
Ka bor sorkar marwei, ki sengtreimon sngewbha, ki nongialam shnong ne hima, ki riew shimet kiba long trai ia ki jaka khlaw  kin nym lah satia ban pynurlong ia ka jingjop ha katei ka bynta tang ma ki.
Ka donkam ka jingkitkhlieh bad  jingiashim bynta kaba ryntih jong ngi iwei pa iwei ban kiar na ka jingpynjot pathar ia ki dieng ki siej da kaba sumar ia ki, kumba ki longshwa manshuwa ki jong ngi ki lah iohi lypa ia ka jingdonkam ki khlaw ki btap da kaba pynneh pynsah ia ki lyngba ki law kyntang, law khang bad ki khlaw ba la buh da ki tnat sorkar bapher bapher ha kine ki sngi.
Ngi donkam ban sngewthuh ba ki jingtreikam ki jong ngi kiba man la ka sngi ki ktah ia ka mariang haba pynjaboh ia ka, kumta ngi donkam ban long kiba phikir khnang ba ngin lah ban jop bad weng ia kita ki jingeh baroh.
Kyrmen ba ka jingrakhe ia ka sngi pynneh pynsah mariang mynta u snem ha ka 5 tarik u Jylliew halor ka mat pdeng “Beat Air Pollution " ba kumno ngin ioh ia ka lyer kaba khuid ba ngin ring mynsiem kan long shisha kaba khia thew bad don jingmut ka ban rung ha ka pyrkhat pyrdain ki jong ngi baroh na bynta ka jingmyntoi jong ngi hi ha ki sngi bad por ban wan ym ba ngin shu rakhe pyndep rukom da kaba klet noh ia baroh kito ki tynrai dieng ba ngi thung hynrei ban da sumar sukher ia ki bad kumjuh ruh ban iada ia ki khlaw ki btap kiba lah don lypa da kaba kiar ban pynjot pathar ne thang dusmon ia ki.
Ki bor sorkar ki dei ban shimkhia ban pynshitom da kaba pynhap katkum ki kyndon pynjot mariang ia kito kiba pynkhein ia ki aiñ ïada mariang kum ka Indian Forest Act, 1927, Environment Protection Act, 1986, Wildlife (Protection) Act, 1972, The Water (Prevention and control of pollution) Act, 1974, The Air (Prevention and control of pollution) Act, 1981 , The Factories (Pollution and Pesticides) Act, 1948 bad kiwei kiwei ki kyndon.

SHILLONG: Ka long khubor kaba ai jingkyrmen ia ki briew ki bym don iing don sem kiba thiah miet  ha ki lynti syngkein na ka daw jong ka jingduk jingkyrduh namar ka Sorkar Jylla kan sa pyntreikam ia ki jaka sah miet ne ki night shelter home ha Shillong, Jowai, Tura bad Williamnagar.
Kane ka la urlong na ka daw jong ka jingai mukotduma ne Public Interest Litigation (PIL) da u Bah Khroolamsalanki Pariat pyrshah ia ka Jylla Meghalaya ha ka High Court jong ka Jylla Meghalaya.
Katkum ka jingkular bala ai da ka Sorkar Jylla lyngba ka Joint Secretary jong ka tnat Urban Affairs ha Iingbishar ha ka Sngi Nyngkong  mynta ka taiew la iathuh ba ka jingpynheh ia ka jaka rieh tngen por miet ne ka night shelter home kaba don ha ka mala ba nyngkong jong ka Shillong Municipal Board (SMB) ka la sdang bad ka kam ka la iai shait shait.
Shuh shuh ki jingai ia ki tiar ki tar kiba donkam kum ki jingthiah, ki pyrda, ki tusok, ki shuki, ki miej sha ki jaka rieh tngen por miet bala don lypa hapoh jong ka SMB la sdang bad yn sa la ban pyndep hapoh 30 tarik u bnai Jylliew mynta u snem.
Katba ka jingshna ia ka jaka rieh tngen por miet ha Jowai la dep pura bad mynta dang leh ia ka jingring bording kaba kumno kumno kan bam por shi taiew bad hadien kata yn sa ai lut ia ki jingdonkam baroh khoit.
Haba iadei ba ka Williamnagar, la bthah ia u Deputy Commissioner ban thaw lad thaw lynti kumno ban pyntreikam ia ka jaka rieh tngen por mietbashipor ha kino kino iing sorkar.
Kane ka jaka rieh tngen por mietkan treikam ha kawei ka quarter sorkar ha DC Colony kaba don san kamra bad ia kane ka iing la aiti ban pyniaid da ka Williamnagar Municipal Board bad ki jingdonkam baroh khoit yn sa pynpoi sha Williamnagar.
La bthah ia ki lai tylli ki Municipal Boards kata ka Shillong, Jowai bad Tura ban phah ia ki jingdonkam jong ki na bynta katei ka jaka rieh tngen por miet bad ka sorkar kan sa khmih biang bad leh ia kaba donkam sah ka 30 tarik u bnai Jylliew.
Ka Sorkar Jylla lyngba u nongiasaid ain jong ka, ka la ai ia ka jingkular ba ka Sorkar kan shimkhia ban pyndep ia kane kam  bad ai ia ki jingdonkam na ka bynta kane ka jaka rieh tngen por miet ban pyniaid da ki Municipal Board hapoh 30 tarik u bnai Jylliew mynta u snem.
Halor ka jingkular jong ka Sorkar, ka Iingbishar ka la pynkut noh ia katei ka PIL bad ka la ong ruh ba lada u nongujor u shem ba don kano kano ka jinglehsting da ka sorkar u la ban ujor biang.
JOWAI: Ka West Jaiñtia Hills Taxi Owner & Driver Association (WJHTODA) kala pyllait paidbah ïaki sticker jong ki taxi kamai ha ophis treikam jong u District Transport Officer (DTO), West Jaiñtia Hills District haka sngi ba ar.

Ïa kine ki sticker lah ban ïoh na u secretary ka WJHTODA naduh ka 22tarik Jymmang 13 tarik Jylliew.
Shuwa ban pyllait paidbah ïa kitei sticker u DTO Ma Ricky Tariang ula kyntu ïaki nongniah bad trai  taxi ba kin long ki nuksa ïa kiwei kiwei ki nongniah kali kamai ban pynbiang ïaki kot ki sla kali bad ban bud ryntih ïaka aiñ niah kali.
Ka WJHTODA manla u snem ka pyllait ïa kine ki sticker sha ki nongniah taxi kamai kiba biang ki kot ki sla bad kamai ha sor Jowai khnang ban khanglad ïa ki briew kiba shim kabu ban kamai khlem kot khlem sla.
Ïa kine ki sticker la tah haka ïit ba hakhmat ki taxi kiba don bad ki number ban pynsuk ïaki nongshong kali bad ki paidbah ban kynmaw lada don mano mano ki nongniah kali kiba iaid lait iaki aiñ niah kali.

SHILLONG: Ka HYC Mawlai Circle kala ïoh ban plie paidbah ïaki artylli ki kamra klass jong ka skul Mawlai Umjaiur LP & UP School haka sngi nyngkong.
Ïa kane ka skul la pynshna da ka HYC Mawlai Circle ha kine ki khyndiat bnai ba ladep.
Ha kane ka sngi la iadonlang ki dkhot jong ka Managing committee(MC), ki kmie ki kpa jong ki khynnah skul, U Rangbah Shnong bad ki nongkitkam jong ka Durbar, ki dkhot ka HYC Mawlai circle kumjuh ruh ki nongiarap jong ka seng.
Ki Nonghikai bad ki dkhot ka MC haba ai jingkren ki la pynpaw ka jingkmen bad ai ka jingiaroh ia ka HYC kaba la iarap ia kane ka skul lyngba kine ki 2 tylli ki kamra klass, ki la kren bynniaw ruh ia la ki nongmihkhmat kiba la leh matlah haba ki peit ia kane ka skul.
La iathuh ba ia kane ka skul la sdang 40 snem mynshwa lyngba ka iing shong wai, sha ka sem masi bad mynta ka la long kume kumba ka long.
Kumba long ki khynnah baroh kiba pule ha kane ka skul kim donkam jingsiew ei ei ruh em lait noh tang ki skul uniform ba kin hap thied hi.
Ha kane ka sngi ki nongiarap ia ka seng ki la ai sngewbha ruh kumba 100 tylli ki shatri sha ki khynnah jong kane ka skul.
U Bah Donboklang Kharlyngdoh President HYC Mawlai circle haba ai jingkren nyngkong eh u la pynpaw ka jingsngew nguh ïa U Blei Nongbuh Nongthaw uba la don ryngkat bad ka seng ha kine ki saw snem ba ladep, bad ngi la pyrshang ban ai ka jingshakri kaba bha tam ia u paid ka bri.
U la kyntu ia ki khynnah bad ki nongpyniaid skul ba kin long kiba trei shitom, khnang ba kane ka skul kan ioh ban sei ia ki riewkhraw kiba long kum u khlur u ban tyngshain ym tang ha kane ka dong ka thain hynrei ha ka Ri baroh kawei.
U la kyntu ruh ia ki khynnah ba kin kiar na ki jingmlien kiba sniew bad ka pep skul shiteng por.
La ioh ruh ka jingkren na iwei i khynnah skul i ba la kyrpad ia ka Managing Committee bad ia ki bor ba halor ba la donkam kyrkieh ban kyntiew kyrdan noh ia kane ka skul na ka klass VIII sha ka klass IX bad ter ter shaduh klass X.
La pynshong shit ia kane ka prokram lyngba ki jingrwai bad jingshad na ki khynnah bad Nonghikai jong kane ka skul.

Kumba yn shu pynkynmaw ka Supreme Court ka la rai ban shah shalan ïa u dewïong bala dep tih lypa, uba don ba palat 75050 metric ton napoh ka Jylla bad kane ka jingailad kan long tang naduh 17 tarik haduh ka 31 tarik Jymmang bad tang halor ki challan kiba naduh u Nohprah 4, 2018.

JOWAI: Na ka daw jong ka jinglehshiliang khmat jong ka tnat Directorate of Mineral Resources (DMR) jong ka sorkar jylla, ka jingangnud jong ki nongkhaïi dewiong ban bteng biang ia ka jingkhaii dewiong naduh lashai ka sngi ka lah ban thud namar ka ophis treikam jong katei ka tnat ka la kyntait ban pynthymmai ia ki challan jong ki.
Kumban shu pynkynmaw ka Supreme Court kala rai ban shah shalan ïa u dewïong bala dep tih lypa, uba don ba palat 75000 metric ton napoh ka Jylla bad kane ka jingailad kan long tang naduh lashai 17 tarik haduh ka 31 tarik Jymmang bad tang kiba la ioh ia ka challan mynshwa kin ioh ban shalan ïa u dewiong.
Hynrei ka ophis treikam jong ka tnad DMR kaba don ha Jowai kam shym la treh ban pynthymmai biang ia ki challan jong ki nongkhaïi bad haduh mynta ka dang pynthymmai ia ka challan tang jong u hynmen u minister u ma Kyrmen Shylla kata u Bison Shylla bad u bah Tuifill Shadap, la kynnoh ki nongkhaii bad ki sengbhalang na rilum Jaiñtia.
Kane ka jingleh jong katei ka tnad ka la pynbitar ia ki nongkhaïi bad sengbhalang.
Ka Ïingkashari kala buh kyndon ïa ka Sorkar Jylla ba kan pynthikna ba ym dei shuh ban don ka jingshalan dewïong ne ka jingtih dewïong da kaba shim kabu na ka jingai jingbit ban shalan haduh 75050 metric ton bad kane ka jingai jingai jingbit ruh ka dei tang halor ki Challan bala dep ban ai.
U Tuesday Lytep, President FKJGP Jaiñtia Hills ula pynpaw ka jingpyrshah kaba jur bad dawa na ka tnad DMR ban kan shimkhia ban pynbeit mardor ïa kane ka rukom ai shalan khnang ban ïa myntoi lang baroh u nongkhaii ym tang ki katto katne ngut.
Ki nongialam ka AJSU, HSU, HYC kila ong ba kitei ar ngut ki briew kiba ioh ban pynthymmai ïa ki challan na ka bynta ka 35 hajar metric ton u dewiong kam dei satia na ka NGT list.
Ka jingioh Challan kine ki arngut ka dei tang namar ba ki don ka jingiajan bad ki briew sorkar bad la kynnoh ba yn die rem dor pat sha ki paidbah nongkhaii.
Ki la byrngem ban ujor PIL pyrshah ia ka tnat halor kane ka jingiuhroit ia ka hok jong kiba bun balang bad leh shiliang khmat ia ki.

U Senior Medical Officer, Ummulong CHC Dr. M Lamare u la ong ba um shym la beh ia ki nongthiah pang, hynrei ka daw ka long namar ka jingbym don um ha kane ka CHC, kumta baroh ka Hospital ka la sma iwtung bad u la phah leit noh ia ki sha ïing namar u ong baka rukom shitom ne pang jong ki nongpang ba don ha katei ka sngi ka biang lada ki mih ruh bad dih tang ki dawai kiba u la ai, ban ia kaba ki sah hangne kin ioh pang shuh shuh tang na ka daw ka jingsma.

JOWAI: Ka jingbymsuidniew jong ka sorkar Meghalaya ha kaban peit ïaka jingeh ki paidbah ha khappud Meghalaya Assam kala paw tynkreiñ haka sngi Balang ha ka shnong Lapangap, ka shnong kaba don ha khappud West Jaiñtia Hills District bad West Karbi Anglong District, Assam ha kaba ka sorkar kam shym la phah satia ïa uno uno u magistor ne u gazetted police officer ban iasaid ïaka jingpyrshah ka sorkar Assam ïaka jingshna surok shnong jong ki paidbah nongshong shnong ka Lapangap.
Ki nongshong shnong ka Lapangap, ka shnong kaba jngai kumba 12 KM na Khanduli kala rai ban maramot ïaka surok na Lapangap sha Khanduli (Kaba iaid lyngba ka shnong Langkeroi kaba hap haka West Karbi Anglong District), hynrei ki Pulit Assam kila wan ban pynsngeh haka sngi Nyngkong namar ba kim shym la pyntip sha ka bor synshar district ka West Karbi Anglong.
Hynrei ka Dorbar Shnong Lapangap kala shim ïaka rai ba la kumno kumno kin bteng beit ïaka jingshna ïaka surok kaba khohruh khohram ban suk ka iaid ka ieng ki kali motor bad u paidbah haka sngi ba Ar hadien ba ki pulit Siatsama Police Outpost kila ong ba kiin wan ban iadonlang ban synran ïaka jingtrei surok jong ki.
Kumta ki paidbah ka shnong Lapangap kila mih paidbah sa shisien haka sngi Balang ban shna ïaka surok khyndew kaba dap da ki thliew ki syar ban lait ki kali motor ban btuid bad ban sahkut haka aiom slap.
Kane ka surok ka dei kaba kaba la iehshrah ka sorkar Meghalaya da ki phew phew snem mynta.
Ki kynhun Pulit Saitsama OP bad Nartiang PS kaba ialam da ki Officer in Charge kila wan sha katei ka shnong, kumjuh ruh u MDC Barato Mukroh Aibor Shadap bad MDC Mynsngat Khanduli u Dawan Lyngdoh kila wan sha katei ka shnong hadien ba u paidbah ula pyntip ban don ka jingtrei ïa katei ka surok.
Hadien katto katne por bala ïaid ka jingtrei surok ki paid nongshong ka Lapangap, ka kynhun pulit jong ka Assam kaba la hiar da ki 2 tylli ki trok ryngkat ki tiar ialeh hapoh ka jingïalam u Border Magistrate West Karbi Anglong, Assam Robert Tualor, DSP P Gogoi bad kiwei kiwei kila wan sha katei ka jaka mar mar ban pynsangeh ïaka jingtrei surok.
U Robert, “Ngi wan hangne ban pynsangeh ïaka jingtrei namar ba ngi la ïoh ka jingujor na ki nongshong shnong ka Langkeroi ba ka don ka jingshna surok khlem ka jingpyntip sha ki bor district jong ki arliang mamla ka West Jaiñtia Hills District bad West Karbi Anglong District.
"Ki Pulit Nartiang bad u Waheh Chnong Lapangap kila pynshai ha u border magistrate ka West Karbi Anglong ba kam don kano kano ka jingshna surok, hynrei ka tang ka jingmaramot surok shuwa ban sdang ka aiom slap ban suk ka iaid ka ieng kali kaba ki shait trei paidbah manla ka snem.
Kumta u Magistor ka Assam ula bthah ïa u Waheh Shnong ka Lapangap bad Goanbura ka Langkeroi ban pynbeit para maki.
Watla u magistrate u kwah ban pynsangeh ïaka jingtrei surok shipor haduh ba kila dep ban pyntip sha ki bor district jong kli arliang mamla, hynrei ki arngut ki MDC bad ki paidbah ka Lapangap ki kwah bad dawa ban bteng ka jingmaramot iaka surok bad ka sur u paidbah kala jop.
Haba kren bad u nongthoh khubot u Robert ula ong, " Ngi ailad ba ki nongshong shnong ka Lapangap kin trei ïa kane ka surok namar ba ka dei ka jingtrei mon sngewbha u paidbah, hynrei lada dei ki skim sorkar ki bor district lane ki sorkar arliang mamla kumba la iakut kin hap ban ïapyntip mar kylliang namar ba kane ka jaka ka dang hap haka jingiakhajia pud.
JOWAI: Ki nongialam jong ka Society for Environment Protection and Sustainable Protection (SEPSD), hynnin ka sngi 14.05.2019, ka la leit ban iakynduh ia u myntri badei peit ia ka koit ka khiah bad kiwei u Bah Alexander L. Hek, ban dawa pynkynriah noh ia kawei ka kharkhana saiñ rnga dewiong kaba la tip kum ka Abhi Coke, kaba don ha Mookhep East Jaiñtia Hills District, ha shwa ban poi Ladrymbai.
Ka seng haka dorkhat ba la ai ha u bah Hek, ka la kdew ba kane ka kharkhana (Abhi Coke) kaba don harud u surok bah bad marjan bad ka Good Shepherd Secondary School, Mookhep, ka la pynmih ka lyer sniew bad ki jaboh na ki pum pum ne tdem kane ka kharkhana kaba ktah ia ka koit ka khiah jong ki nongshnong shnong bad ia ki khynnah jong kane ka skul.
U President SEPSD Wanbun Dkhar u la ong ba kane ka kharkhana kaba don hangne kala treikam mynta da ki bun bun tylli ki snem, kaba la wanrah ka jingeh bad ka jingma kaba khraw ia ki paidbah bad ia ki sawdong sawkun jong ka mariang, kumjuh ruh kane ka  kane ka kharkhana ka la iaid lait ia ki aiñ ki kyndon ba iadei bad ka mariang bad kane ka kharkhana ka dei ban jngai  naki shnong ki thaw ne na ki jaka paidbah.
Na ka liang ka SEPSD ka kyntu  ia u myntri ka koit ka khiah ban kynriah noh mardor ia kane ka kharkhana sha kiwei pat ki jaka kiba jngai naka shong ka thaw ne ki jaka pule, namar kum kine ki jait kharkhana ki pynmih shibun ka tdem kaba sniew kaba ktah ia ka koit ka khiah jong ki briew kiba don sawdong kane kharkhana.
KA SEPSD kala ai jingtip ruh ia kane ka jingdawa pynkynriah ia kane ka kharkhana,  sha U Deputy Commissioner East Jaiñtia Hills District, Divisional Forest Officer (T) Jowai, Directorate of Commerce and Industries Government of Meghalaya, Shillong, Chief Forest Officer JHADC bad sha u Member Secretary Meghalaya State Pollution Control Board.

JOWAI: Ki lai tylli ki sengbhalang kiba kynthup ia ka All Jaiñtia Student Union (AJSU), ka All Jaiñtia Hills Social Welfare Organisation (AJHSWO) bad ka Hynniewtrep Youth Council (HYC) kila leit buh da ka dorkhat ha u Deputy Commissioner ka West Jaiñtia Hills District haka 7 tarik une u bnai ban ujor halor  ka jingjur palat ka jingshalan tuh iaki masi manla ka miet sha Bangladesh.
Kane ka jingshalan tuh ia ki masi sha Ri Bangladesh kala ktah ruh ia ka dor jong ka dohmasi hapoh rilum Jaiñtia na ka daw jong ka jingduna masi bad u paidbah ula ud halor ka jingrem dor jong ka dohmasi.
Naka liang kine ki lai tylli ki sengbhalang haka miet 6 atrik kiila leit hi dalade ban jurip haka surok Jowai-Amlarem-Dawki  bad ha katei ka miet ha ka por kumba 9:30 PM kine ki nongialam seng kila lap da ki phew phew tylli ki trok kit masi ki iaid lyngba u surok Jowai-Amlarem-Dawki kiba kit masi bad la suba jur ba ki dei kiba shalan beaiñ sha Bangladesh.
Shuh shuh la ong ba ki Challan ba kine ki trok ki ioh ka dei ban pynpoi ia ki masi tang haduh ka shnong Demthring, West Jaiñtia Hills.
Katba kiba bun hi ki trok ki masi ki dei kiba shalan tuh ïaki masi sha Bangladesh.
Ha katei ka miet ki nongialam jong kine ki seng kila pan jingiarap ruh na ki Pulit Amlarem ban bat ia ki ar tylli ki trok ba la phah pynsangeh kiba don ia u Register ML 04-A 8835 bad ML04B 8099, haka jaka ba la pynsangeh ia kine ki trok, la kynnoh ba ki pulit ki la shu ai daw kumne kumtai bad kila shu phah iaid beit ia kine ki trok kaba pynsuba jur ba ki pulit ruh kila lah ban donkti haka kam shalan masi tuh.
Ha ka jingiadei bad kane naka liang u General secretary ka AJSU, PS Phawa u la pyntip ruh sha u SP ka WJH, hynrei haduh mynta na ka liang ki pulit kim pat shem la leh ei ei ruh.
U DC West Jaiñtia Hills hadien bala ioh ïaka dorkhat ula ong ba un shimkhia ia kane ka kam.
Kine ki lai seng kila dawa na u DC ban pynlong ka jingkhynra iaki trok kit ba iaid iaka surok Jowai-Amlarem-Dawki bad ban phah da u magistor bad pulit bad ka kynhun nongring dur ban lap ïaka jingshisha halor ka jingshalan masi beaiñ na kane ka thain sha Bangladesh.
JOWAI: Uwei u samla ba kyrteng u Sonidawan Sayoo uba na ka shnong Mynska ula jahrngai haka por ba u leit khwai naduh ka 5 atrik une u bnai.
La ïathuh ba une u Sonidawan u dei uba pule ha Thomas Jones Synod College haka subjek Honours Khasi 2nd Semester kaba ka exam jong ki kan sdang lashai ka sngi.
La kyntu ba lada don mano mano ba ïohi ïa u sngewbha ban pyntip ha une u number 8787686584.
Ha kawei pat ka khubor u wei u samla ba kyrteng u Ngeitmon Pala (20) uba dang shah hikai kum u Security Guard ha Bosco Pnar Institute, Mihmyntdu, Jowai ula iap ngam jyllop haka thwei Thlumuwi kaba don ha lynti ban leit sha Amlarem.
U Ngeitmon Pala u dei uba na ka shnong Sakhain, East Jaiñtia Hills  District.
Kane ka jingjia haka sngi Balang bad la lah ban sei ïaka met jong u Ngeitmon haka por 5 baje nohphaisngi na katei ka thwei da ka jingiarap ki pulit Fire and Emergency Service.
DAWKI: Ka jingthmu ban tei ïaka Integrated Check Post (ICP) ha Dawki, West Jaiñtia Hills District ka dei ka nusip jot ïaka War Jaiñtia baroh kawei bad kaba sngewlehraiñ shuh shuh ka dei ba ki trai khyndew haduh mynta kim pat ioh ka bai musur khyndew na ka sorkar jylla.
Kane ka ICP kaba dei peit da ka Land Ports Authority of India (LPAI) la plie paidbah ha ka 24 tarik u Kyllalyngkot 2017 bad la mang ban pyndep ha u bnai Nailar 2018 haka jinglut T.92.34 klur haka jaka kaba heh haduh 22 Acres.
Kane ka ICP ka don ha lynti ban leit sha ka shnong Muktapur na Tamabil, hynrei kane ka jingthmu ban tei iaka kad khaii kala sangeh mynta namar bala mih bun bah ki kynram kynram nalor ka jingbym ioh bai musur khyndew ki trai jaka, ka Ri Bangladesh ruh kala phah kynran ïa kane ka ICP na ka jaka ba don kham shadien namar ba kala jan palat sha u pud bad la ong ban kan wanrah ka jingkhapngiah kaban ktah iaka khaii hadpeng ki ar tylli ki Ri.
Ym tang katta ka jingsahkut kane ka jngpyntrei ïaka ICP ka dei ruh ba ka don ka mukotduma ha Meghalaya High Court hadpeng ka TK Engineering kaba shim kontrak ban tei iaka ICP pyrshah sorkar India bad kiwei kiwei namar ba kala shah pyndam trei bad shah ba ka slem ban pyndep iaka jingtrei bad kiwei kiwei.
Mynta kane ka jingbym iaid shakhmat ka jingpyntrei ïaka ICP kala pynkynduh mawsiang ïaki nongshong shnong ka thain War Jaiñtia naduh Tamabil, Amlympiang, Amdoh, Rhongkum, Amsku, Muktapur, Syndai, Hawai Bhoi bad kiwei kiwei ki shnong namar ba ka surok ban iaid sha kine ki shnong na Tamabil kala kylla surok ktieh bad sniew palat liam kaba buh jingeh iaki kali motor bad ki briew ban iaid ban ieng.
Ka jingbun ki trok kit maw, mawsalin khlieh la ka sngi kala wanrah ka jingsahkut kali ha katei ka jaka.
Ki kali rit kim lait ban iaid iaka surok kaba ktieh kaba dap da ki thliew ki syar bad bun sien ki paidbah kim lah ban pynpoi iaki marrep jong ki sha iew bad hap leit phai shala shnong.
Halor kane ka jingsniew ka surok na kaliang ka JSU War Jaintia Circle kala dawa na u nongmihkhmat ka thain bad ka sorkar ban shna noh ïa katei ka surok ban suk ka iaid ka ieng u paidbah.
La dawa ruh na ka sorkar jylla ba kan tuklar ha kaba iadei ban ka jingsahkut ka jingtrei ïaka ICP.
JOWAI: Ki Pulit jong ka West Jaiñtia Hills District kila ioh kurup biang ïaki battery ba shah tuh kiba pyndonkam ha ki tower mobile phone bad kila iohkem ruh 6 ngut ki suba snar nongtuh.
Ki Pulit kila iathuh ba haka sngi Balang haka por 6 baje mynstep hadien ka jingioh khubor kaba thikna, kila leit ban khynra ïa kawei ka jaka sah ki bar jylla kiba die nar jot tin jot kaba don ha Ladthadlaboh, Jowai hajan ka kudam ka Rymbai Gas Agency.
Ki pulit haka jingkhynra ia katei ka ïing ba sah ki bar jylla kila ioh kurup  ym duna ïaki 40 tylli ki battery tower mobile na khrum jingthiah jong ki.
Nalor ki battery la kurup ia kiwei kiwei ki tiar jong kiba battery kiba la dep ban pynpait pynpra bad song ha ki byrni, ki kurat ot nar bad kawei ka kali gypsy jot kaba pyndonkam da kitei ki bar jylla, kaba la pyndait da ka registration number thok.
Kine ki battery dei kiba la shah tuh na Tuber, Thadmuthlong, Jowai bad Hynniawmer bad kiwei kiwei ki jaka.
La iathuh ba ha kane ka jingkhynra ia katei ka iing ki don katto katne ki suba donkit kila lait phet.
Halor kane ka jingiohkurup ia kine ki battery ka jingtohkit ki pulit kala iaid shakhmat bad dang thwet ruh ia kiwei kiwei ki suba ban pynpra iaka kynhun jong kine ki nongtuh.
SHILLONG: Ka St Anthony’s Higher Secondary School, Shillong bad ka BBS College, Shillong kila wan haka kyrdan kaba nyngkong haka resol Higher Secondary School Leaving Certificate (HSSLC) kaba la pynbna da ka Meghalaya Board of School Education (MBOSE) haka science bad commerce streams haka sngi Balang.
Ka Debjanee Bhattacharjee jong ka St Anthony’s Higher Secondary School kala wan haka kyrdan kaba nyngong eh haka science stream bad u Bhanudaya Upadhaya jong ka BBS College haka commerce stream.
Na West Jaiñtia Hills District, ka North Liberty HSS bad ka KJP Synod Mihngi HSS kila ïoh ban buh jaka ialade haka kyrdan first ten position haka HSSLC Science.
Ka North Liberty HSS kala wan haka kyrdan balai bad ba phra bad ka KJP Synod Mihngi HSS haka kyrdan ba hynnriew.
U Berennice Anerict Tang jong ka North Liberty Hr Sec School, Jowai uba sah Dongmihsngi Ladthadlaboh, Jowai ula wan haka kyrdan ba lai bad u Kamphereiei Pala (North Liberty Hr Sec School, Jowai)  uba na Moolamylliang, East Jaiñtia Hills District ula wan haka kyrdan ba phra.
Haka kyrdan ba hynriew la ioh da u Khroo Meda Dkhar na ka skul KJP Synod Mihngi Hr Sec School, Jowai uba shong ba sah ha Chilliangraij, Jowai.
JOWAI: Ka jingkhaii masi tuh sha Bangladesh katba nang mih ki sngi ka nangjur bad tang ha ki ar bnai, ha u bnai Lber bad Iaiong 2019 la ïoh kurup haduh 303 tylli ki masi kiba thmu ban pynkam sha shilliang ïa u pud India Bangladesh.
Kiba bun kine ki masi ba shah kurup ki dei na ka thain Mukutapur BOP kiba hap haka Dawki Police Station.
Dangshen ha u bnai Iaiong 24,  ki shipai ïada khappud BSF kiba na ka Muktapur BOP kila ïoh kurup 13 tylli ki masi na ki 2 tylli ki trok kiba ïaid lyngba ka surok Amlarem Muktapur.
La kem ruh ïaki 6 ngut ki briew kynthup ki nongniah kali, nongbud bad ki suba nongpynkam ïaki masi sha shilliang u pud bad kine ki briew ki dei ki trai shnong na Pdesngshakap, Amlarem, Pynthorlangtein bad na Ri Bhoi.
Shuh shuh haka 21 tarik u Iaiong ki shipai BSF jong ka Nongkhen BOP kila kurup 2 tylli ki masi dab.
Ha kaba iadei bad kane ka jingioh kurup masi la register case ha Dawki Police Station bad la pyngngat haka kyndon ain ba lehbein iaki mrad ki mreng PCA Act.
La bthah ïa baroh ki trai kiba jah masi, shah tuh masi ban wan mih ha thanad ban pyndep iaki jingdonkam ka aiñ.
JOWAI: Ka seng Hynniewtrep Achik National Movement (HANM) Laskeiñ Block Circle, kala kynnoh ba ki Chairman/Secretary Village Employment Council (VEC) hapoh Laskeiñ Block, ki bthah ïaki nongtrei bylla kiba don job card ban pynphai biang ïaka pisa kaba la thep haka account na block sha ka VEC tang namar ki ai kontrak bad pyndonkam da ki kor ban trei ïaka skim Mahatma Gandhi National Rural Employment Guarantee Scheme ne ka skim bylla 100 sngi.
Ka HANM kala kynnoh ba bun tylli ki shnong ne ki VEC kiba don ha Laskeiñ Block ki shim kabu ïa kane ka skim kaba la mang ban ai kam 100 sngi ïa uwei pa uwei u nongshong shnong, pynban haka jaka ban ioh kam ki nongbat job card ki ai kam sha ki briew kiba don ki puh shilum bad kiwei kiwei ki kor kaba pynduh jingmyntoi ïa u paidbah ne nongtrei bylla.
Ka HANM kala kynnoh ba mynta kane ka jingleh jong ki VEC ban bthah iaki nongbat job card ban pynphai iaka ppisa kaba la poi haka account jong ki kala pynkulmar iaki nongtrei shi spah sngi.
U President HANM EJ Law, u la ong ba ia kito kiba ym shym la trei ne bylla ruh hynrei kiba don iaka Job Card, ka pisa ka rung hapoh ka Account jong ki bad ia kine ruh ki VEC ki phah sei ia ka pisa ban leit ai ha kti jong ki.
U la ong ruh ba ka seng kala lap ba kane ka jia ha VEC  Shangpung, Pamanik, Mynska bad kiwei ki VEC ba don hapoh ka Block Laskeiñ.
Ha kaba ki VEC ki lehbor bad pyntrei da ki kor ki bor ïa kane ka skhim bad ki VEC byrthen ba lada ki paidbah kim mynjur iaka jingpyniaid ka VEC kin sangeh ban wanrah jingtrei lyngba ka 100 sngi.
U EJ Law u la ong ba ki VEC, haka jaka ba kin pynshlur ia ki nongbylla ban trei da ki kti ban ioh trei ki nong ioh job card, hynrei ki pyndonkam beit da ki puh shilum da kaba ai kontrak tang ban ioh myntoi ki katto katne hapoh ak VEC.
JOWAI: Ka Seiñraij jong ka Mukhaialong kumba ju long manla u snem, mynta ka kynti ruh kan pynlong ia ka Shad Sukra 2019 haka 11.5.2019 ha ka por 1 baje nohphaisngi ha madan Shad Sukra jong ka shnong.
Ka Shad Sukra kadei ka jinglehkmen shuwa ban hiar bet ïa u symbai u phniang bad ban ainguh ïaka mei mariang ban bha ban miat u kba u khaw.
U Assistant Secretary jong ka Seiñraij Mukhaialong, u Hundred Phawa ula pynpaw ba ka Seiñraij Mukhaialong ka khot u wer sngewbha ia baroh ban wan iashimbynta ha kane ka Shad Sukra ba kan long kaba phuh kaba phieng.
KHLIEHRIAT: U wei u briew uba kam ialade ba u dei u dkhot ka Hynñiewtrep People Defence Alliance (HPDA) ula ngat ei ha ruh nar ki pulit jong ka East Jaiñtia District namar ka jingshah kynnoh dawa pisa na ki dukan ha Khliehdupon, Ladrymbai.
Une u dkhot ka HPDA u dei uba la tip kyrteng kum Andrew Lamare.
La ïoh bat ia u da ki shipai shnong (Village Defence Party) jong ka Ladrymbai Khliehdupon hadien ba kila ioh ka jingujor ba une u Andrew bad ki paralok jong u ki leit ban dawa pisa na ki katto katne ki dukan ha Khliehdupon haka 3 tarik une u bnai.
Mar mar ki shipai shnong kila shimkhia ban wad ia u bad ïoh bat ia u bad aiti syndon sha ki pulit.
Halor kane ka jingshah kynnoh dawa pisa u dkhot ka HPDA ka jingtohkit ki Pulit kala iaid shakhmat.
Nakaliang ka Hynniewtrep Defence Alliance (HPDA) kala kyntait iaka jingkam dkhot une u Andrew bad kala ong ba ym don dkhot uba kum kane ka kyrteng hapoh ka HPDA bad kane ka dei tang ka jingpynthohbria iaka HPDA.
JOWAI: Ki paidbah nongshong shnong jong ka Iooksi, West Jaiñtia Hills kila pynpaw ïaka jingsngew kyndit ha kaba ïadei bad ka jingkiew kynsan jong ka bill light kynthup ïaki longïing ba duk (BPL) bad don ruh kiba ioh pdiang kaba bai bording kaba la kot haduh T.552119.
Ka KSU Laskeiñ Circle hapoh ka jingialam u President u Balawantei Suchiang kala leit jurip dalade haka jaka siew bill light ki nongshong shnong jong ka Iooksi haka sngi Nyngkong bad kala lap tynkrein ïaki jingbakla ha rukom shna bill light ka MePDCL jong ka Khliehriat Sub-Division.
Wat la ki nongshong shnong kila dep siew ïaka, hynrei ka paw ba kim pat dep siew la bun bun bnai (outstanding bill).
Ka bording BPL ruh kaba sam sha ki longïing kiba duk, ka bai bording kala kiew palat iaka T.600.
Ka KSU kala dep ïakynduh bad iakren bad u SDO ka Khliehriat Revenue Sub Division, Khliehriat ban pynbeit ïa kane ka jingthurmur ka tnad, pynban haduh mynta ym shym la pynbeit ïa kane ka jingkhaler ki nongtrei ka tnad MePDCL.
SHILLONG: Ka Hynñiewtrep Youth’s Council (HYC) Mawlai Circle haka sngi Nyngkong kala leit ban khynra ïa ki kot ki sla jong ki nongkhaïi bar Jylla kiba khaïi sla tyrpad bad synsar ha iewdielang ha Mawlai Mawiong (Mawiong Regulated Market).
Ha kane ka jingleit khynra kaba dei ruh lyngba ka “Sier Lapalang Operation" ka HYC kala lap ïa kiba bun ngut ki nongkhaïi bar Jylla kim pat pynthymmai ïa ka Trading License hapoh ka KHADC watla ka por kala kut hynrei la lap ba ki pyndonkam beit da kiba rim bad ka HYC mar mar kala khang khyrdep lut ïa baroh ki dukan bad ki kudam jong ki nongkhaïi bar Jylla tad haduh ba kin da pynbiang bad pynthymmai ïa ka Trading License.
Ka HYC kala lap ruh ba ki don ki nongbylla kiba trei ha katei ka jaka kim don ïa ka Labour License bad ïa kine ruh ka seng kala phah sangeh noh.
Ka HYC kala leit ban ïakynduh ruh ïa ka Secretary badei peit ïa kane ka ïew ban ïakren ha kaba ïadei bad ka jingïoh lad jong kine ki Bar Jylla ban khaïi bad trei ha kane ka jaka khlem ki kot ki sla kiba biang.
Ha kane kajuh ka sngi ka HYC Mawlai Circle kala leit ban khynra ruh ïa ki kot ki sla jong ki nongbylla bar Jylla kiba trei ha ka jingkieng jong ka surok by pass ïa kaba la pyntrei da u Bah Bungsing Sohphoh bad hadien ba ka HYC kala jurip ïa ki kot ki sla la lap ba baroh na kine ki nongbylla bar Jylla kim don ïa ki kot ki sla kiba biang khamtam ïa ka Labour License napoh KHADC, kumta ka HYC kala pynher krad lut ïa baroh kine ki nongbylla bar Jylla sha ka jaka kaba ki wan.
U Bah Maiñbor Khyriem u la ïathuh ba hadien ka jingioh jingujor ba ki don ki nongkhaïi ki ba khaïi laitlan khlem da pynthymmai ïa ki kot ki sla ha katei ka jaka kumta kala pynlong ïa ka seng ban leit khynra bad la lap ba la jan baroh na kine ki nongkhaïi kiba khaïi lyngba ki kot ki sla ba la kut por.
Ka HYC lyngba ka Sier Lapalang Operation kan ym shong kli kti, hynrei kan ïai khynra na ka por sha ka por ïa baroh ki nongkhaïi bad nongtrei bar Jylla bad dawa ruh na ka Sorkar ba kadei ban pyntreikam noh mardor ïa ka ILP hapoh ka Jylla Meghalaya khnang bah lah ban teh lakam ïa ka jingwan rung kynthlep jong ki bar Jylla.
KHLIEHRIAT: Ka  Khasi Students’ Union (KSU), Narpuh Circle haka sngi Nyngkong kala leit hiar haka kharkhana dewbilat  Dalmia Cement Bharat Limited kaba don ha Thangskai East Jaiñtia Hills ban pynsangeh mardor iaka jingthmu pynrung kyrteng Aadhaar ïaki spah spah ngut ki bar jylla kiba trei bylla ha katei ka kharkhana.
Ka KSU kala kynnoh ba la leh sop sop ïaka jingpynrung kyrteng Aadhaar hapoh katei ka kharkhana bad la suba jur ba ka don eiei sha lyndet bad ka KSU kala phah pynsangeh mardor ia kane ka jingpynrung kyrteng Aadhaar  namar ba bun na ki bar jylla ki dei tang ki nongbylla sngi kiba wan na Assam bad kiwei kiwei ki jylla bad kim bym don satia kino kino ki kot ki sla ban pynthikna ba ki dei ki nongshong shnong ka Ri India.
Katba na kaliang ki nongtrei katei ka kharkhana kila kam ba ka jingthmu ban pynrung kyrteng addhar ka long tang na ka bynta ki nongtrei ka kharkhana, da kaba kam ba lada kim don aadhaar kim ioh ban sei ia ka Provident Fund  jong ki.
U Ma Kwillness  Suchiang President ka KSU Narpuh Circle ula ong ba naka liang ka KSU kan nym ailad satia iaki bar Jylla ban ioh pynrung kyrteng Aadhaar ha katei ka thain , lada ki donkam Aadhaar kila dei ban leit pynrung kyrteng sha shnong trai lajong.
Kane ka jingleh ka kharkhana dewbilat ban pynrung kyrteng sop sop ia ki nongtrei bylla barjylla ka buh ka jingma kaba khraw ia ka thaiñ bad ka jaidbynriew namar bun na kitei ki poiei dei kiba wan na ri Bangladesh, Assam bad na kiwei kiwei ki jylla bymdon ki kot ki sla ba biang, ula ong u nongialam ka KSU u Ma Kwillness Suchiang.
Ka KSU kala maham ïa kane ka kharkhana ban sangeh ia kane ka jingleh tuh ban kdup ia ki poiwir bad  lada kan lap biang kan pyni da ka kam.
“Ka Assam ka dei ka ktem ki khar Bangladesh, ki sah tang katto katne sngi ha katei ka jylla ki ioh epic, pan card, nangta ki wan bsuh khlieh sha ka jylla jong ngi da kaba leh mynleh wad kam bylla, hynrei ki kam pat da kumwei," la ong Deibormi Dkhar General Secretary KSU Narpuh Circle bad ula bynrap ba dei halor kane ka nongrim ba ki pyrshah namar ba kim kwah ba katei ka thain kan shah tyllep ha u poiei shisngi.
JOWAI: Kiba ha ïing hasem jong u khynnah 14 snem ka rta,  u Asuk Ryngkhlem kila pyntip ba la lap ia u ha ka sngi Saitjain na kawei ka tandoor shet jingbam ha Riatturiem, Jowai.
U Asuk Ryngkhlem, ula jah na ïing ba u sah ha Iawmusiang Jowai naduh ka 28 Iaiong naduh ka por kumba 7 baje janmiet bad la ujor ruh ba ula jahrngai.
La iathuh ba la lap ïa une u khynnah na kane ka dukan shet jingbam bad ula trei bylla ha katei ka dukan khlem iathuh ïano ïano ha kiba ha ïing bad ula shu mih la mih na iing.
K a Special Assistance Grant ba ai bhah ka Sorkar Kmie ha KHADC kam dei ban poi sha ka pla jongno re jongno bad ban pyndonkam bakla ia kane ka pisa, hynrei dei ban pynpoi hok sha u paidbah.
Ka KHADC ha kine ki snem kiba la leit kala paw ha ka jingshna ia ki aiñ iada Ri ki ban iada ia ka jaidbynriew Hynniewtrep.
Hynrei tang 2 bnai ba wan ki MDC thymmai ngi iohi pynban ba ki ia knieh iaka song pisa SAG ka sorkar kmie bad kane kalong kaei kaei ka bym lah ban pdiang bad kane ka dei ka jing ñiewbein ia ka jingangnud jong ka jaidbynriew na ka KHADC.
Ka jaidbynriew ka angnud na ka KHADC ba kan wanrah ki aiñ ban iada ia ka jinglong ba kyrpang ka jaidbynriew, ka riti dustur, ka khyndew ka shyiap, dorbar trai ri bad ban bud dien ia ki aiñ kiba la dep thaw kum ka Khasi Lineage Bill bad kiwei kiwei ki aiñ.
Ka HYC kala ong ba EC thymmai khamtam ka tnad Trade bad Labour kila shimkhia ban trei na ka bynta ban tem bad ban khanglad iaka jingkamai spah beaiñ u barjylla, hynrei  sngewsih ba ki don pat kiba bunkam ha ka ia knieh pisa bad ia knieh shuki.
Ka jingshlur jong kine ki MDC ban ia knieh pisa bad ia knieh shuki imat kadei na ka daw ba ki dang thmu bad ki sngew ba ki lah ban hukum ia ki officer ka council ban kin thep ia ka pisa paidbah ha ki account shimet jong ki, kumba la kynnoh ba mynshwa ba u CEM (Bah P N Syiem ) u la hukum ia u secretary ka KHADC  ban shim ia ki pisa ka professional tax ban thep ha ki personal account bad ban ia pyndonkam bakla ia ka pisa lyngba ka Monolith festival bad kiwei.
Ngi lyngngoh ba haduh mynta ka police department kam pat lah ban pyndep wat tang ia ka investigation halor kane ka kam.
Ka jing bym pat pynshitom ia u nonghukum bad nongleh ia kane ka kam beain ban thep Pisa ha ki personal account bad ki nong pyndonkam bakla ia ki Pisa ha ka monolith festival ka pynlong ia ki MDC Mynta ban ia khieh ia kane ka pisa da kaba mutdur ba kin ioh thep ha ka pla lajong.
Ka HYC ka dawa bad maham ia baroh ki MDC ba ka pisa lyngba ka Special Assistance Grant kadei ban poi sha ki paidbah ym ha ki account jongno re jongno kumba long mynshwa.
Ngim tuklar mar katno phi ia sam hynrei ki dei ban pynthikna ba kan poi hok sha ki paidbah.
Ngin buddien ban pynthikna ba wat tang shityngka na ka pisa ba la mang ban pyndonkam ymdei ban rung ha ka personal account jongno re jongno.
Ka seng ka kyntu ruh ia baroh ki MDC ba ki dei ban ia pynleit jingmut ban iada ia ka jaidbynriew ha baroh ki liang  da kaba wanrah bad shna ia ki ain bapher bapher bad ki polisi treikam bapher bapher ym ban ia bunkam ha ka jingiaknieh pisa ne pynkhyllem shuki.
Ngi kyntu ba phi ia shna ia aiñ iada Ri  ym ban ia knieh shuki.
Ka jaidbynriew ka donkam ia ki nongshna aiñn ban iada ia ka Ri ym ia kiba rhah shuki.
Roykupar Synrem General Secretary HYC, CEC.
JOWAI: Ka Jaiñtia Students Movement (JSM) Central Body kala dawa na ka Jaiñtia Hills Autonomous District Council (JHADC) ban phiah noh ia ka Elaka Jowai bad ban khynra bad pyndam ïaki Trading license jong bar jylla.
Ha ka dorkhat sha u Chief Executive Member (CEM), JHADC ma Thombor Shiwat, ka JSM kala pynpaw ba ka Elaka Jowai ka kynthup ia ki 83 tylli ki shnong kiba hap hapoh West Jaintia Hills bad East Jaintia Hills District bad  27 tylli ki shnong ki hap hapoh Raid Tuber.
U Leningstar Rymbai President ka JSM, ula ong ba ki nongialam jong kitei 27 tylli shnong naduh u snem 2016 ha u bnai Risaw 7 tarik hapoh ka lama jong ka Raid Tuber Elaka Demand Committee ha Tuberkmai Shnong, East Jaiñtia Hills District kila pynpaw ba kala dei ban phiah noh iaka Elaka Jowai bad ban thaw iaka elaka Tuber.
Ula ong ba ka ka lah ban thaw ia ka Elaka Tuber katkum ka aiñ Jaintia Hills Autonomous District (Establishment of Elaka and Village and Election, Appointment, Powers, Functions and Jurisdiction of Dolloi/Sirdar and Waheh Shnong) Act 2015.
Ka JSM kala dawa ruh ban wanrah biang iaka jinglong tynrai ka Iaw Pynkat kaba don ha Khliehriat East Jaiñtia Hills ba ka kam die jingdie kanlong tang hapdeng Khasi Pnar bad ban pyndam mardor ia ka jingdie jingdie jong ki bar jylla kiba la jyllei katba nang mih sngi kaba la ktah ïaka ioh ka kot jong ki trai ri.
La dawa ruh ban khynra ia ki dukan bar jylla ba ki suba jur ba kin don ki kot ki sla ba biang ban khaii pateng bad ban shongdie jingdie ha katei ka iew.
Ka JSM haka dorkhat kaba la ai ha u CEM kala dawa ban buh tnad treikam ka JHADC ha Khliehriat ban pynsuk ïa u paidbah bad ba ki MDC ruh kin wan shisien shi taiew khnang ba kin paidbah kin lait ban leit shaduh Jowai ban leit pyndep kam ha ophis Jowai.
Ka JSM ka la dawa ruh na ka JHADC ban khynra trading licenses bad labour licenses ba jyllei ki bar jylla bym don kot don sla kiba khaii pateng, buh dukan sha kane ka thain kaba la ktah pat iaki trai ri hapoh 15 Jymmang 2019, lym kumta kan shim da kiwei ki rai.
U CEM u la bthah iaka JSM ba ki dei ban wanrah ia ka shithi kaba la soi da ki nongialam shnong jong ki 27 tylli ki shnong hapoh Raid Tuber kiba kyrshan ia kane ka jingdawa.
Ha kaba iadei bad ka jingkhynra Trading License bad labour License pat u CEM ula kular ban shimkhia bad ban buh ïaka tnad treikam ka JHADC ha Khliehriat, u CEM ula  kular ban rah ia kane ka mat ha ka jingialang jong ka Executive Committee.

Ka um kaba wan na tyllong um ka shnong na Amkru kaba don shajan ki par tih mawshun kham pajih na New Nonglamin kala kylla um ktieh bad ka bor shnong kala pyntip sha ka PHE ha kaba na kaliang ki Engineer ka PHE, SDO, JE kila wan ban jurip bad pynthikna ba kam bit ban pyndonkam ïaka um ban dih bad kala pynsangeh iaka jingsam um shapoh shnong.

SHILLONG: Kum shi bynta ban kyntiew ia ka rukom sumar Khasi ha ka jylla la plie paidbah ia kawei ka jaka ai jingsumar ba la tip kyrteng kum ka Mebaai Tribal Health and Wellness Centre ha Golflink Shillong bad la plie paidbah ia kane ka jaka sumar da i Kong Serina Wahlang, iba long i Kongsan haka sngi Palei.
U Myntri ka tnad ka koit ka khiah u Bah AL Hek ba dei ruh u MLA ka Pynthorumkhrah constituency ula shimkhia bha ban pynioh ia kane ka jaka ai jinsumar Khasi bad Ayurveda.
Kane ka jaka ai jingsumar la seng ruh ha ka jingiatreilang bad ka Vasudeva Vilasam na Kerala ban ai jingsumar ia ki paidbah lyngba ka Ayurveda bad kumjuh ba ki paidbah kin ioh ia ka jingsumar Khasi (Traditional Khasi Massage).
Haba ai jingkren ha katei ka sngi la ka liang u Bah Hek u la ong ba kane kan wanrah ia ka jingai jingsumar kaba kham pher sha ki paidbah ha kaba ka rukom sumar Ayurveda kan iaid lang bad ka rukom jingai sumar Khasi.
U la ong ruh ba ki nongshong shnong ka Golflink ki ba kot ia ka 70 snem ka rta lane ki ba la palat ia kane ka snem kin hap ban siew tang ia ka bai pynrung kyrteng kaba dei 10 tyngka hynrei baroh ka jingai jingsumar kan long kaba um donkam ban siew pisa shuh.
La ong ruh ba kane ka jingiatreilang kine ki ar tylli ki rukom sumar kan wanrah ia ka jingmyntoi ia ka jylla Meghalaya kaba don ia kumba palat 3000 tylli ki kynbat (medicinal herbs and plants) bad kumjuh ka jingdon bun ngut ki nong sumar Khasi.
U la ong ruh ba kane ka jingiatreilang da kaba ai jingsumar Ayurveda bad jingsumar Khasi kan khring ruh ia ka jing jngohkai pyrthei lyngba ka koit ka khiah (health tourism) bad kumjuh yn lah ruh ban kyntiew ia ka rukom sumar Khasi.
Na ka liang u Dr. Pradeep Jyoti na Kerala u la pynpaw ba ia kane ka rukom ai jingsumar Ayurveda la sdang ha bun tylli ki jaka hikai naduh u snem 1884.
U la ong ruh ba ka don ka jingthmu ban kam pynbha shuh shuh ia ki rukom shna dawai kynbat na ka bynta ki jingpang ba ha rukom bad kumjuh ruh ban kyntiew ia ka jingsumar Khasi kham shajrong.

Ka khubor pulit ka ïathuh ba ki runar kila kawang da u petrol bomb ha phyllaw ka FCI kaba la wanrah ka jingjulor ïa ki trok kit khaw ba don u registration number AS 01 DC 6297 bad AS 01 CG 9187, hynrei ka jingsmat ki  ki pulit pynlip ding la lah ban tem ïaki thylliej ding ban pur sha kiwei kiwei ki trok.
