SHILLONG: Ka North East Forum for Indigenous People (NEFIP) kan pynlong ia ka jingialang pyrkhat kam kaba nyngkong eh ha ka 30 tarik une u bnai ha Nongbah Shillong.
Ka NEFIP kadei ka synjuk ki sengbhalang na ka thaiñ Shatei Lammihngi kaba la seng ha Imphal Manipur ha une u bnai Iaiong.
Na Jylla Meghalaya ka Confederation of Meghalaya Social Organization (CoMSO) ruh ka ïasohlang bad ka NEFIP.
Ha ka jingialang kaba long ha Imphal, Manipur, ka NEFIP kala shim katto katne ki rai kiba kongsan, kata ban pyrshah ia ka Citizenship Amendment Bill, ban pyrshah ruh ia kino kino ki aiñ ki ban iohlong nongshong shnong ka Ri India ïa ki bar ri.
Ka NEFIP kan ialeh pyrshah ia ki polisi treikam ka sorkar Kmie lada ki ktah mationg ia ka jinglong tynrai ka jaidbynriew kane ka thain, ka kyndew ka shyiap bad ki hok kyrpang ki trai Ri trai muluk.
Ka NEFID kan kyrshan ruh ïa ki sengbhalang na ki jylla bapher kiba dawa ia ki aiñ kum ka Inner line permit system bad kiwei ki aiñ ban iada ia ka jingioh rung bad sah ki mynder ha ki jylla bad kane ka synjuk ki sengbhalang kan long ka kynhun kaban ieng iada bad kyntiew ia ki trai muluk ha ka dong ka thain hi baroh kawei.
SHILLONG: Ki runar kiba ym lah satia ban ïthuh kila thang ïa ar tylli ki trok kit mar ka Food Corporation of India (FCI) ha Mawlai Mawroh, Shillong hynne shiteng synia.

SHILLONG : Ka kynhun ki katto katne ki nongthoh khubor na nongbah Shillong ryngkat ka jingsynñiang u Bah Banteidor Lyngdoh, Myntri sorkar jylla ba dei peit ia ka tnad Sports & Agriculture bad MLA na Mawkynrew Constituency, ha ka 27 tarik u Iaiong, ka la hiar sha ka shnong Kharang ban ai jingiarap sha ka skul Angels’ Space kaba dei ka skul ai jinghikai ia ki heprit ha ki class Pre-Primary lane Kindergarten.
Kane ka skul kaba san snem mynshwa la mut ban pynduh noh namar ki skul Pre-Primary lane Kindergarten ym shym la pynhap ha ka thup jong ki skul ba bei tyngka da ka Sarva Shiksha Abhiyan (SSA).
Hynrei ka jingshim khia na ka liang ki kmie ki kpa, ki nonghikai bad ki riew don mynsiem ki la pynieng ia kane ka skul kaba ai jingnang jinghikai kumba 40 ngut ki khynnah mynta.
Ia ka kynhun la lam khmat da ki nongthoh khubor ba la kham rangbah ba kynthup ia u Bah David Laitphlang, President ka Shillong Press Club, u Bah Joe Thangkhiew, u Bah Reigning L Mawphlang, u Bah D Banjop Mukhim, uba dei u dkhot ka bor pyniaid jong kane ka skul ha kane ka shnong lem bad kiwei kiwei.
Na ka kynhun ki nongthoh khubor ka la iarap noh synniang ruh sha kane ka skul da ka pisa.
Kane ka skul ka don tang ar ngut ki nonghikai bad lai ngut pat kiba shu wan iarap hikai.
Shuh shuh na ka liang ki nonghikai kane ka skul ki la pynpaw ka jingai khublei ia u president ka ka SPC uba kham ha shwa u la dep noh synniang sha kane ka skul da ka Wall TV kaba la iarap ia ki khynnah ban kham lah ban pyn-iar shuh shuh ia ki jingtip lyngba ki video na ka YouTube bad kiwei kiwei.
Kumba long mynta kane ka skul ka long kaba i sangsot ban peit khlem da ia kren khamtam ha ki por slap, haba ki don tang ar kamra kiba rit bad la ker da ki lyntang dieng bad sop da ki tin.
Hynrei watla katta ki heprit ha kane ka sngi ki la pynpaw ka jingsngew kmen bad ai ka ka jingshad pdiang burom ia ki dkhot na ki nongthoh khubor ha kane ka kamra long skul.
Hadien kane la pynlong ia ka jingialang kaba lyngkot ha kaba la ioh jingkren na i Headmistress kane ka skul, I Kong W Mynsong, iba la pynpaw ka jingai khublei ia ki nongthoh khubor bad na ka bynta u synniang uba ki la noh.
U Bah David Laitphlang, u la ong ba kum kine ki skul ki dei ki shlem ban sara ia ka jingnang jingtip sha ki heprit ba dang lung bad ai khublei ia ki bor pyniaid skul, ki nonghikai bad kumjuh ia ki kmie ki kpa kiba ai ka jingiatrei lang wat hapdeng ki jingeh ban pynlong ia kane ka skul ban nang kiew sha khmat.
U Bah D Banjop Mukhim, u la iathuh khana lyngkot shaphang ka jingsdang kane ka skul ha kaba ma u lem ka ïing ka sem jong u ki la ai ka kti kamon ka kti ka diang ban kyrshan ia kane ka skul ryngkat ka jingiatrei lang ki kmie ki kpa bad ki nonghikai.

SHILLONG: Ka rukom ai jingsumar bathymmai kaba la tip kyrteng kum ka Stem Cell therapy ka la kylla long ka jingkyrkhu bah u heprit Ethan Nongbet ba 8 snem namar u la ioh ia ka jingkoit jingkhiah hadien ba u hap mad ia ka jingshitom kaba jur ha ka met ka phad jong u haduh ba shipor ka la pynkhuslai shikadei eh ia ki kmie ki kpa jong u.
U heprit Ethan la kha ia kum u khyllung uba koit ba khiah hynrei ynda u la kynjoh ia ka rta kaba 7 bnai u la ioh kem kynsan ia ka jingpang Pneumonia bad u la shem jingeh ban ring bad pynhiar mynsiem bad ki hap ban leit rah sha hospital ar sien shi snem tad haduh ban da kynjoh ia ka rta kaba 4 snem, iathuh I kong Ivoreen Nongbet.
Lai snem  kynthih, i heprit Ethan u la sdang ban ioh kem ia ka jingpang kaba ktah ia ka met baroh kawei.
Ha ka rta kaba 7 snem u la shem jingeh wat ban iaid bad ka jingkhia ruh ka la nang hiar arsut.
Hadien ba la leh ia ka CPK test la pynthikna ba une u heprit u la ioh ia ka jingpang ha ki shyieng (Muscular Dystrophy) naduh u Nailar, 2018.
Hadien ba la pyndep ia ki Test baroh, la pynthikna ba i heprit Ethan i ioh ia ka jingpang, Duchenne Muscular Dystrophy.
Ki doctor ki la bthah ia i Kong Ivoreen ban sumar lyngba ka Stem Cell Therapy bad lyngba ka jingpeit ia ki video lyngba ha YouTube, I la pdiang ia kane ka rukom sumar.
La rah ia u Ethan sha NeuroGen BSI ha u Naiwieng 2018 bad leh ia ka jingsumar NRRT (Neuro Regenerative Rehabilitation Therapy).
Dei lyngba kane ka jingsumar, u heprit Ethan u la lah ban ioh jingkoit suki pa suki lyngba ka jingsumar bad ka jingiarap da ki Physiotherapist, Occupational Therapist, Psychological Counsellor bad kiwei kiwei.
Ka NeuroGen Brain and Spine Institute, kaba don ha ka sorbah Mumbai kaba long kawei na ki jaka sumar bapawkhmat ha ka ri India ha kaba iadei bad ka jingpang ha ki shyieng (Stem Cell  Therapy) kaba don ruh ia ka Rehabilitation Centre.
Ka ai jingsumar ruh lyngba ka Stem Cell Therapy kum ha ka jingpang Autism, Cerebral Palsy, Mental Retardation, Brain Stroke, Muscular Dystrophy, Spinal Cord Injury, Head Injury, Cerebellar Ataxia, Dementia, Motor Meuron Disease, Multiple Sclerosis bad ka jingpang Meuropsychiatric.
Haduh mynta, kane ka shlem ai jingsumar ka la lah ban pynkoit  palat 8000 hajar ngut ki nongpang na ki 60 tylli ki ri.
Ki la wan iakynduh ruh ia u Myntri Rangbah, u Conrad K Sangma bad ia u Secretary ka tnat ka Koit Khiah ka Sorkar Jylla, u Pravin Bakshi na ka bynta ban pan jingbit ban pynlong ia ka Medical Camp ha kane ka nongbah Shillong khnang ba ki longiing kiba duk kin ym donkam satia ban leit shah sumar shaduh Mumbai," ong ka Head Surgical Services jong ka Neurogen Brain & Spine Institute ka Dr.
Risha Bansod ha ka jingiakynduh bad ki lad pathai khubor hynne ka sngi palei ha nongbah Shillong.
Ka Dr.Bansod ka la iathuh ba dei ka NeuroGen BSI ka jaka sumar ia kine ki jait jingpang ha ka pyrthei baroh kawei.
Ka NeuroGen Brain and Spine Institute kan sa pynlong ia ka Medical Camp bad ka OPD Consultation Camp ha ka 28 tarik mynta u bnai ha sorbah Guwahati, Assam na ka bynta ki nongpang kiba shong basah ha ka thaiñ Shatei Lammihngi jong ka ri India.

JOWAI: Ka All Jaiñtia Youth Welfare Organisation (AJYWO) kala kam ba katkum ka jubab RTI kaba kala ïoh ba ki don tang 1397 ngut ki bar jylla kiba don Trading License ha baroh kawei ka Rilum Jaiñtia.
Kine ki barjylla kiba biang ki kot ki sla (Trading License) ba kila ioh na ka Jaiñtia Hills Autonomous District Council (JHADC) ban khaii pateng bad ban buh dukan kilong kumne harum: Ladrymbai-508, Khliehriat-387, Jowai- 257, Hawkers-42, Coal/Cement-48, Umkiang-33, Dkhiah-38, Mynkre-20, Sookilo-17, Thangskai-12, Nongsning-8, Jalaphet-5, Moopala-4, Byndihati-2, Chiehruphi-6, Tongseng-10.
“Ngim lah ban pdiang ïa kane ka jingkhein kaba la ai da ka JHADC namar ba katkum ka jinglong jingman hi ha Rilum Jaiñtia khlieh la ka sngi la wan kiew ki bar jylla na kylleng ban khaii pateng.
Ka jingduna ki Trading License ba pyllait da ka konsil ka dei ka jingbym pyntreikam hok ïaka  aiñ khaii pateng ki barjylla-The Jaintia Hills Autonomous District (Trading by Non-Tribals) Regulation (Act)-2011", la ong u nongialam ka AJYWO U MH Dkhar bad ula bynrap ba ki bun bah ba ki bar jylla kiba bym don license kiba wan khaii hapoh u pud u ang ka konsil, hynrei namar ka jingbym larkam ka tnad Taxation JHADC, ka khajna kaba ka konsil ka dei ban ioh ka lait ei shabar ka pla jong ka.
Ha u bnai Naiwieng 26, 2018 ka AJYWO, hadien baka la ïoh jubab RTI kala ai dorkhat sha ka konsil ban dawa ban peit bniah halor ka jingai Trading License bad Non-Tribal Employees’ Service License ha ka Ri Jaiñtia bad la kyntu ban ai license sha ki nongkhaii bar jylla tang haki jait kam ba ki ki trai jylla kim lah ban pyniaid.

Wah Nangbah Junction (No Entry): Hadien ka  por 3 PM  baroh ki kali kiba wan na New Hill Point bad na Wah Nangbah ym shah ban rung lyngba ka surok ban leit sha  DC ophis lait noh ki kali jong ki briew elekshon bad kiba rah kor EVM kiba lah ban rung sha Nangbah Stand.
HK Singh Junction (No Entry): Ki kali kiba wan na kaliang Chutwakhu bad Mission Compound  ym shah ban rung lyngba ka surok sha DC Office bad ki dei ban iaid lyngba ka surok ban poi sha Jrisaleiñ Chutwakhu, Mynthong haduh Stand War lait noh tang ki kali elekhson bad ki briew elekshon.
DC By Pass Junction (No Entry): Baroh ki kali kiba wan lyngba ka surok stand War kila lah ban iaid na ka surok nadien ka DC ophis bad bam mih ha lad wah Nangbah.
Seiñraij Parking Lot (No Entry): Ym shah ia baroh ki kali  kiba wan na  kane ka surok sha Iawmusiang lait noh ki briew elekshon bad ki kali elekshon.
Thomas Jones Junction (No Entry): Ki kali paidbah bad shimet kin hap ban iaid lyngba ka surok ban rung sha Thomas Jones Synod College bad ki mih sha surok Dulong College Road.
Nangbah Stand: Tang ki kali elekshon kiba wan na New Hill Point kiba lah ban ieng ha Stand Nangbah bad hadien bala dep pynhiar  ïaki kor EVM bad briew elekshon ki lah ban ieng haka jaka ieng kali ka Ummulong, Amlarem-Dawki Stand bad ha madan Jrisaleiñ.
Dawki Road: Ki kali elekshon kiba wan na ka thain  War Jaiñtia ne Dawki Jowai Road shah ban rung bad pynieng ha surok ban leit sha JHADC bad haiden bala dep pynhiar ïaki briew elekshon bad kor EVM  ki lah ban pynieng kali ha Amlarem Dawki Stand , Mynthong sha jan Library bad madan Jrisaleiñ.
Baroh ki kali pulit, Civil Zonal, Sector ki lah ban iaid lyngba ka surok iawmusiang sha DC ophis bad ym shah ban pynieing kali ha DC Point haduh ka surok ban rung sha SP Ophis.
Ban lain a ka jingkhapngiah ki lah ban buh ki kali ha jaka pynieng kali ki kali war, Ummulong bad Jrisaleiñ.

Ka jingthmu jong ka NGT ban oh ia kane ka khajna na u dewiong ba shallan bad dep tih ka long ban pynbha pynmiat ïa ki mei mariang kaba la shah pynjulor na ka kam tih dewiong ha ka jylla.

JOWAI: Ka Confederations of Meghalaya Social Organisations (CoMSO) ka la leit ban iashim bynta ha ka 1st North East People Conference 2019 ha Imphal, Manipur.
Ha kane ka conference hadien ka jingiathir jingmut sani bha halor ka jingeh jong ki trai ri trai muluk jong ka thain Shatei Lammihngi la thaw ïa kawei ka forum kaba kynthup lang ïa baroh ki seng trei mon sngewbha kaba la ai kyrteng ka North East Forum for Indigenous People (NEFIP).
Ïa kane ka conference la pynlong da ka Manipur People’s Against Citizenship (Amendment) Bill, 2016 (MANPAC) ka seng kaba kdup lang ha kawei ka lama ïaki 84 tylli ki seng ban pyrshah  ïaka CAB ha jylla Manipur naduh 1 tarik haduh 3 tarik une u bnai Iaiong kaba la wan ban ïashimbynta da ki sengbhalang bapher bapher ka thaiñ  Shatei Lammihngi lait noh ka Sikkim.
Ka kynhun  jong ka CoMSO kala leit ïashimbynta ha katei ka conference haka jingïalam u Chairman CoMSO, u Bah Robertjune Kharjahrin uba long u President ka HYC ha ka jingdon ryngkat ki Nongialam jong ki seng bapher bapher kiba don hapoh ka kynhun jong ka CoMSO.
Ha kane ka jingialang nyngkong eh, ki sengbhalang bapher bapher jong ka thain Shatei Lammihngi kila iakynduh lang ha kawei ka jaka na ka bynta ban ia thir bad ia mir jingmut halor ki jingeh bapher bapher kiba ki trai ri trai trai muluk ki iakynduh na ka por sha ka por.
Ha kine ki lai sngi ba la pynlong ia kane ka Conference lai iatai bad iathir sani bha kumno ban wanrah ia ka jingiatylli hapdeng ki sengbhalang jong ka thain bad ruh ban pynpaw ia kawei ka sur kaba tylli lang mlon ha kino kino ki khep kiba ki nongshong shnong ka thain ki ia kynduh jingeh.
Da kawei ka jingmut la rai ban thaw ia ka synjuk ki Sengbhalang ka thain Shatei Lammihngi ia kaba la ai kyrteng ka North east Forum for Indigenous People (NEFIP).
La jied Convener jong ka Core committee ia u Ningthouja Lancha na Manipur bad 3 ngut ki nongmihkhmat na kawei ka jylla kum ki dkhot kane ka Core Committee.
Ia ki nongkitkam ba pura yn sa jied ha ka jingialang jong ka core Committee ka ban sa long shen ha Shillong.
Ha kane ka conference da kawei ka sur la shim ban pyrshah ia ka CAB, la rai ban pyrshah ia baroh ki polisi treikam ka sorkar India kiba ktah mationg ia ka thymmei ka bat khyndew bat shyiap, ka hok kyrpang, ki riti dustur jong ki trai ri trai muluk jong kane ka thain bad kane ka synjuk kan kyrshan ia baroh ki sengbhalang ha ka thain kiba dawa ia ka ILP System, NRC bad kiwei ki aiñ iada jingrung kyrthep ki mynder ri hapoh ka jylla.

Ka jingduh ka bording ha katei ka thain kalong kaba man ka sngi kaba wanrah ka jingeh kaba khraw ia ki paidbah nongshong shnong naduh ki khynnah skul kiba don ha ki jingpule, ki PHC, bad ka jingduh nong kaba khraw khamtam ia kito kiba pyndonkam da ka light ia ka  jingshet bad jingtrei jingktah jong ki.

“Haka shisngi ngi ioh light tang 20 minit, hynrei ym tip na kaei ka daw ba thud ka bording haba ym donkam jingmaramot ne duh ki line ha katei ka thain," ong u Bah Minot.
Une u rangbah ula kynnoh ba ka ka MeCEL ka ai bor ding tang sha ki cement factory kiba don ha thain Narpuh bad ka pynduh pat ïa u paitbah nongshong shnong.
Ka NBAJAC ka kyntu ia ki bor pyniaid jong ka MeCEL kidei ban pynbiang ia ka bor ding ha ka thain Narpuh bad lada ym lah ban pynbiang ding kin shim da kiwei ki rai kiba tyngeh.
U Daiapherbha Lamare uba long u Secretary ka NBAJAC, ula ong ba ka Load Shedding ka treikam naduh 9:00 PM haduh 12:00 AM ha Narpuh, hynrei ka MeCEL kala shim kabu shaba palat da kaba pynduh bording palat iaka por kaba ka pynbna ha ka shisngi ha katei ka thain.

JOWAI: Ka Shnong Rymbai, East Jaiñtia Hills District kala shah jied ha ka Sorkar India kum ka ‘Digital Village’.
Ka Shnong Rymbai kadei kaba nyngkong eh ba shah jied na East Jaiñtia Hills District kum ka Digital Village kaba ki nongshong shnong kila pyndonkam ïaka kor Computer bad Internet.
Ha Meghalaya ki don 11 tylli ki Digital Village bad ha Rilum Jaiñtia ka Raliang bad Rymbai ki dei ki ar tylli kiba la ioh ka nam ‘Digital Village’.
Ka Shnong Rymbai, da ka jingshah jied kum ka ‘Digital Village’, ki paid nongshong shnong kin ïoh shuh shuh ka lad jinghikai  ha kaba iadei  bad ka Computer course, ki jingthep form online, ka jingtreikam ki Bank, ki Solar Light LED,  ka jinghikai skul lyngba ki digital technology bad kiwei kiwei de ki kam lyngba ki Common Service Centre.
Ka sorkar pdeng kala buh thong ba ha kine ki shi snem ban wan lyngba ka Ministry of Electronic and Information Technology kan jied shi lak tylli ki shnong ban pynkylla kum kita ki Digital Village ha Ri India.
Ia ka Shnong Rymbai la jied ryngkat ka jingïatreilang ka Kong Releaseme Sympli, VLE (Village Level Entrepreneur) jong ka Digital Seva CSC Rymbai.
Kum ka dak ban lehkmen ïa kane jingioh nam Digital Village ka shnong Rymbai, la pynlong ïaka jingïalang haka jingïadonlang u Ma Justice Lyngdoh, Waheh Shnong Rymbai uba pyniaid ruh ïaka jingialang, u Ma Lincoln Nixon Dkhar, Kyrmen Chyrmang na SBI (Ladrymbai Branch) uba la batai shaphang Financial Inclusion (Ka jingiadei u paidbah bad ki bank haka jingim ba man la ka sngi ban kynshew pisa bad khaïi).
Kiwei kiba ïadonlang Ma Elios Swer, Dalloi jong ka Elaka Rymbai, U Ma Helpman Phawa bad  Kong Regina Sympli, District Manager CSC E- Governance Services India Ltd bad ruh I Kong Releaseme Sympli ka VLE jong ka Rymbai CSC, U Bah Joshua H. Lyngdoh  State Head jong ka CSC E- Governance Services India Ltd, uba la pynshai ïaki jingmyntoi ba ïoh lyngba CSC bad ula kyntu ïaki nongshong shnong ba kin ia treilang bad ka CSC khnang ba ki shnong ki thaw kin myntoi.
La sam ruh ïaki khusnam sha ki nongiashim bynta haka “Run for Unity", PMGDISHA certificate bad PM-SYM.

MOOSAKHIA: Ka Society for Urban and Rural Empowerment (SURE) kala pynlong ïaka training kaba shibnai lynter halor ki rukom rep bad rukom ri jingri ba bunjait hakajuh ka jaka.
Ïa kane ka training kaba shibnai lynter la pynlong ha ka shnong Moosakhia kaba don hapoh ka Amlarem Sub Divsion jong ka West Jaiñtia Hills.
Ïa kane ka training la plie pyndonburom daka kong B. M. Majaw kaba long ka District Horticulture Officer (DHO) jong ka West Jaiñtia Hills haka 25 tarik jong u Lber haka jingïadonlang ki nongïalam ka SURE, u Waheh Chnong bad ki nongïalam shnong.
Haka jingkren lamkhmat jong u, u H. H. Mohrmen ula batai ba kane ka training ka dei kaba la kyrshan da ka Meghalaya State Skill Development Society (MSSDS) halor ka projek Supporting Human Capital Development in Meghalaya Package #21 Under SFC.
Kane ka Training ka dei halor ka Integrated Farming (Small Farmers) kaba hikai ïa ki rukom rep bad rukom ri jingri naka bynta ki nongrep ki bym da don eh ka jaka kaba heh.
Ha kajuh ka por kane ka projek ka ïarap ruh ha kaba ïa dei bad kaban pynïaid ïew ïa ki mar rep bad kumjuh ruh ban shna ne pynmih ki kynja jingbam na ki jingrep kiba ki nongrep ki pynmih.
U Mohrmen ula ong ruh ba ha kane ka training nalor kaba hikai ïa ki rukom rep babun jait bad ki rukom ri jingri, yn hikai ruh ïa ki rukom shna sboh, shna dawai khniang, ri ngap bad wat ban rep tit ruh.
Ka kong B. M. Majaw haka jingkren jong ka ka kyntu ïa ki nongrep kiba bun ruh na ki, ki dei ki samla bad kin shim khia ïa kaei kaba la ai training ïa ki bad ban pyndonkam pat ïa ki.
I pynkynmaw ruh ba ha kane ka pyrthei kyrduh kam, ki samla kila dei ban khmied sha ka kam rep ne ka kam ri jingri kum ka lad ïohkam ïahjam.
Ila pynkynmaw ruh ïa ki nongrep ban a ka liang jong ka sorkar kala sangeh ban ai ki sboh dawaiphniang sha ki nongrep, kumta ila kyntu ruh ïa ki ba kin pyndonkam da ki sboh khlem dawai bad ban sdang ruh da ka rukom rep Organic namar ka ïew mynta ka dawa ïa kine ki jait jhur.

JOWAI: Ka shnong Raliang, West Jaintia Hills District, ka la shah jied ha ka sorkar India kum ka Digital Village ba nyngkong eh ha West Jaiñtia Hills District.
Ha Meghalaya ki don 11 tylli ki Digital Village bad ka Raliang kadei kaba nyngkong eh ha West Jaiñtia.
Khyndiat shaphang ka Digital Village, ka mut ka Shnong ba ban treikam beit da ki Computer ha kiba bun ki liang ne kata ka e-Governance, kaba ki paid nongshongshnong kin pyndonkam beit da ka internet ne online haba kiba bun ki bynta.
Kane ka jingshah jied ka Raliang kum ka Digital Village, ka sorkar kan kyrshan ïa kane ka Shnong da kaba ka free training halor ka jinghikai Computer nangta pyndonkam WI-FI, nangta ki jingthep form online, ka jingtreikam ki Bank, ki Solar Light LED, ka jinghikai skul lyngba ki digital technology bad kiwei kiwei de ki kam lyngba ki Common Service Centre.
Na ka liang ka sorkar pdeng ka la buh thong ba ha kine ki shi snem ban wan lyngba ka Ministry of Electronic and Information Technology kan jied shi lak tylli ki shnong ban pynkylla kum kita ki Digital Village ha ri India.
Ïa ka Raliang la jied da ka jingtrei shitom U Ma Pyndap Lamare, VLE jong ka Digital Seva E- Governance CSC Raliang.
Kane ka jingshah jied ka Shnong, ka la pynkmen shibun ïa ki paidbah jong ka Shnong , la pynlong ïa ka jingïalang kum ka dak ban plie ïa kane ka Digital Village ha kane ka jingialang la ai jingkren da I  u Ma S. Sanki Lamare Waheh Shnong Raliang uba dei ruh u Chairman.
Kiwei kiwei kiba kren ki kynthup iaka  N Shylla iba dei I Branch Manager jong ka SBI (Raliang Branch), Joshwa Lyngdoh  State Head jong ka E- Governance CSC ,I kong Ameecia Pariat District Manager E- Governance CSC.
La ïadonlang ruh ka kong Morngait Lyngdoh VLO jong ka SHG,Block, U Ma Chawas Lyngdoh Dolloi Elaka Raliang.
JOWAI: U Kyrtong monlang jong ka Meghalaya Democratic Alliance (MDA) u Dr. Jemino Mawthoh ula ong ba dei ka Congress party kaba sdang ban khang bam doh masi bad ka symbol jong ka Congress mynshwa ka dei ka “Masi" bad dei ka sorkar Congress kaba sdang ban iasaid ban pynkylla ia ka Citizenship Amendment Bill (CAB).
Ka dei ha ka por ka jinglong Prime Minister ka Indira Gandhi ba ka la hukum ia ka ki myntri rangbah jong ki 14 jylla ban khang bam doh masi bad dei ha ka por u Manmohan Singh kum u Prime Minister ba la iakren ban wanrah ia ki amendment ia ka CAB, ong u Dr Jemino haba kren haka jingïalap elekshon ba nyngkong eh jong u ha rilum Jaiñtia ha Iongpiah, Jowai mynta ka janmiet.
Ula ther tyngeh ia u kyrtong jong ka Congress u Ma Vincent H Pala uba ong ba ha ka elekshon MP dei ban jied tang ia ki National Party namar u MP na ki party riewlum lada un shah jied un  long kumban jngi ha ka duriaw baheh.
U MLA barim jong ka Nongthymmai u la pynkynmaw ia ki paidbah ba ki ladep phah ia u Prof G G Swell kum u MP san sien bad u la iakhun ia ka elekshon na ka party rilum bad u Prof Swell u la leh ki kam kiba radbah na ka bynta ka jaidbynriew.
Ula ong ruh ba u ma Pala u dei uba sniewbok tam namar ba ym lah ban pyllait ïaka jingkhang tih dewiong haka jylla bad kum u MP ka Jylla ha kine ar samoi ym shym la lah ban pynioh kam ïaki samla pule kiba la nang la stad bad kam don ruh ka jingpyrshang ban plie lad plie lynti iaki ba kin pynpaw ïaka sap ka phong jong ki.
U Dr. Jemino u la pynshai paidbah ba lada u ieng na ka symbol monlang ka pyni bad u dei kyrtong shimet bad kan nym don kano kano ka jingteh jingkhum ia u bad lada u jop u la ban rung sha kano kano ka party.
U la ong shuh shuh ba u la ieng na ka symbol UDP hadien ka jingiamynjur lang jong ki nongialam jong ki party hapoh ka MDA khnang ba kan don ka jingteh ka jingkhum ia u hadien ba u la jop ia ka eleshon MP.
“Lada nga poi sha ka thong nga peit ïa ki mat kiba ktah iaka jylla, kata ban pynbeit ia ka jingiakajia khappud, ka jingpynrung ia ka ktien Khasi ha ka Eighth Schedule, ka roi ka par bad ban iakhun ban pyllait ia ka jingkhang tih dewiong ha ka Jylla nalor bad plie lad lynti ïaki samla ba don sap ban ieng hala ki jong ki kjat", la ong u Dr. Jemino Mawthoh.
Halor ka jingpyntreikam jong ka MP Skim lada u poi sha ka thong, u Dr. Jemino u la ong ba namar u long u kyrtong monlang jong ka sorkar MDA te kumta yn thaw ia ka committee kaba kyrpang haba yn don ki nongialam na ki seng sain hima sima kiba don ha MDA ban khmih ia ka jingpyntreikam jong ka MP Skim khnang ba baroh ki constituency ban pynpoi hok sha u paidbah.
Haba ai jingkyrshan kaba pura ia u Kyrtong jong ka sorkar MDA, u Myntri ka tnat Transport u Ma Sniawbhalang Dhar ula kyrpad ia ki paidbah ba kin ai ia ka vote ka jong ki ia u Dr. Jemino bad ka jinpynieng ia u Dr. Jemino na ka symbol UDP bad na Tura ban iakhun da ka NPP kaba ka kyrtong ka dei ak Agatha Sangma kadei kaba la pynbeit da ka MDA.
Kiwei kiwei kiba la ai jingkren ki long u Chief Executive Member jong ka JHADC u Ma Thombor Shiwat, u Chairman ka JHADC u Ma Lakhon Biam, ki MDC kiba kynthup ia u Ma Saron Pasweth, u Ma Phasmon Dkhar, u Ma  Brightstar Chyrmang haka jingiadonlang u Bah Moonlight Pariat u President ka UDP West Jaintia Hills bad u Ma O Lamin u President jong ka NPP West Jaintia Hills.

JOWAI: Ka elekshon sha ka ïing dorbar thawaiñ Lok Sabha ka la nang nang shongshit shuh shuh hadien ba ka seng Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) ka la rai ban jied ia u MLA ka Shillong South u Bah Sanbor Shullai kum u kyrtong na ka 1-Shillong Parliamentary Constituency.
Ka party ka la pynbna ia ka kyrteng jong u Bah Sanbor kum kyrtong hynnin ka miet ha Delhi ha ka second list bad ka la hap ban jied napdeng lai ngut ki briew kiba applai tiket kynthup ia u Bah Sanbor bad ki ar ngut kiwei pat ki long u Bah E Mawrie u vice president jong ka BJP jong ka jylla Meghalaya bad u Bah Lakhon Kma u nonghikai jong ka North Eastern Hills University.
U Bah Sanbor un iakhun ia kane ka elekshon pyrshah ia u Bah Vincent H Pala uba long u MP ba mynta uba long u kyrtong ka Seng Indian National Congress bad ia u kyrtong monlang jong ka Meghalaya Democratic Alliance (MDA) u Dr. Jemino Mawthoh bad u kyrtong ka Khun Hynniewtrep National Awakening Movement (KHNAM) u Bah T H S Bonney.
Ka party BJP wat la ka donlang hapoh ka lama jong ka MDA hynrei ka la kyntait ban pdiang ia ka rai jong ka ban pynieng tang ia u Dr. Jemino kum u kyrtong monlang bad ka la iaid shakhmat ban pynieng ia u Bah Sanbor kum u kyrtong jong ka.
U Bah Sanbor u la jop ia ka elekshon  MLA naduh u snem 2008 ha ka por ba dang tip ia ka Shillong South Constituensy kum ka Laban bad um pat ju rem ha ka eleshon MLA haduh mynta.
U MLA jong ka Shillong South u dei u khun jong u Bah S Khongwir (bam kwai ha dwar U Blei) bad u don mynta 52 snem bad u shong u sah ha Kench Trace, Shillong.
JOWAI: U MDC jong ka Mynsngat Khanduli Constituency u Ma Dawan Lyngdoh u la ong ba ka Nartiang constituency ka dei kawei na pdeng ki constituency kaba sah dien tam hapoh ka jylla ha kaba ia dei bad ka roi ka par, ka pule puthi, ka rep ka riang, ka koit ka khiah, ki jaka kynshew pisa (bank) bad kiwei kiwei.
Une MDC u la ong ba ka pule puthi ka long kaba kordor tam ha kane ka juk mynta, hynrei haba ianujor ïa kane ka thain bad kiwei pat kiba don hapoh ka jylla kam iahap shuh khamtam naduh Mynsngat Khanduli kim don ki jaka pule kaba biang katkum kane ka juk lait noh ki skul private hynrei haba phai sha ka juk stad mynta kine ki jaka kim lah ban ai ka jinghikai kaba biang ia ki samla jong kane ka thain.
Ula ong ba bun ki khynnah samla kim ioh lad ban pyndep ia ki jingpule jong ki namar ba katei ka thain kam don centre iakhun eksamin.
Ban ïakhun eksam selection bad matrik jong ki, ki hap ban mih na shnong ban leit thoh shaduh Ummulong kaba jngai haduh 40-50 Km na ka shnong jong ki, kane ka jing jngai ka la pynlong ia shibun ki samla ban sangeh ban bteng ïaka jingpule jong ki, ha ka juh ka por na ka daw ka jingduh jingkyrduh kim ioh lad shuh ban leit pyndep ia ki jingpule tang na ka daw ka jingjngai.
Ha kaba iadei bad ka koit ka khiah, ka thain Namdong Khanduli ka la shah ieh khunswet haduh katta katta namar shibun ki nongpang ki ba dei ban sumar hapoh Namdong PHC ki la hap ban leit sha duh Nartiang PHC, Jowai lane Shillong tang na ka daw ka jingbym don ki doctor man ka sngi bad ka jingduna dawai bad ki nurse hapoh kane ka PHC.
Ka Namdong PHC kaba la dei ban kyntiew kyrdan sha ka CHC naduh u snem 2012 bad ia ka Khanduli sub centre sha ka PHC hynrei kaba sngewsih ban iohi haduh mynta u snem khlem lah ban leh eiei.
Halor kane ki nongshong shnong jong kane ka thain ki la mad shibun ki jingeh ha ka pang ka shitom hynrei ym don nongiarap ban pynsuk ia kane ka jingeh u paidbah.
Ka jingjngai jong ki shnong na kawei ka sub centre sha kawei pat kam iahap shuh katkum ka jingbun briew (population) bun ki jaka kiba la don ar shah ia kaba dei ban don kum ka Namdong Sub Centre kat kum ki kyndon jong ka health department ka jingbun briew ha kawei ka sub centre ym dei ban palat ia ak 3,000 lai hajar ngut hynrei kumba ka long ha Namdong mynta ka la don palat 7,000 (Hynniew hajar ngut) kum juh ka Sanaro Sub Centre, Khanduli Sub Centre bad kiwei kiwei ki sub centre kiba don ha kane ka PHC ki long kum juh.
Kane ka la pynlong ia ki nong shong shnong ban duh ei shibun ki mynsiem ba kordor tang na ka daw ka jingbymbiang ki jaka sumar katkum ba ki dei ban don.
Ha kaba ia dei bad ka C&RD Block kaba la mut ban plie naduh u snem 2014-15 ha ka shnong Namdong ha kaba wat ia ka jaka la dep ai sngewbha sha ka department ban pynsuk ia ki briew kane ka thain, hynrei haduh kane ka por kam pat urlong satia wat lada ki paidbah ki la dei ban ioh ruh haba ia nujor katkum ka jingjngai bad ka jingbunbriew kane ka thain.
Une u MDC thymmai ula ong ba ka shong hok ban ioh ia ka C&RD Block ha Namdong namar tang na ka daw ka jingjngai jong kane ka C&RD Block ki paidbah bun sien ki la duh ei ia ki jingmyntoi kiba ki dei hok ban ioh khamtam ia ki nongrep namar ki la hap ban pynlut por da ki sngi ban leit khamtam naduh Lapangap Khanduli ki la hap ban leit da ki 100Km ban poi sha Block kaba don ha Thadlaskein, kane ka ka jingjngai bad ka jingbun briew ha kane ka C&RD Block kala pynshitom ia ki paidbah nongkyndong jong kane ka thain ha kaba ia dei bad ki jingmyntoi kiba ki dei ban ioh ha ki bynta bapher bapher.
Ha kaba ia dei bad ka bank ka shnong Namdong kaba kynthup naduh Mynsngat shaduh Sanaro ka la dei ban don ki bank hapoh kine ki jaka khnang ban pynsuk ia ki paidbah jong kane ka thain ha kaban jingkynshew ia ka pisa tyngka khamtam ha kane ka juk mynta kaba la donkam Ia u wei pa u wei ban don ia ka bank passbook na ka bynta ki jingdonkam jong u hynrei kine baroh ki la sahkut tang ha ki jingiakren khlem da poi shano shano kane ka la pynduh nong ia ki paidbah jong kane ka thain jong ngi.
Une u MDC ba dang shah jied thymmai ula pynpaw ka jingbynniaw halor kane ka jingsah dien ka thain bad ula khot ula wer ïaki paidbah ban iatreilang khnang ban wan ka roi ka par ha katei ka thain.
N a ka liang ka CoMSO  (CoHSO bad ka AGHJAC)  ngi kwah ban pynshai ba na ka liang ka kynhun ka dawa ia ka Inner Line Permit system (ILP) ha baroh kawei ka jylla Meghalaya ban  teh lakam ia ka jingrung kyrthep bad ioh buhai shnong laitlan ki poiwir ha ka jylla Meghalaya.
Naduh ba sdang ngi la dawa ba ka sorkar Meghalaya ka dei ban pyntreikam ia ka Bengal Eastern Frontier Regulation Act, na ka liang ka sorkar ka la pynshai ba  naduh bala weng noh ia ka Garo hill na ka Bengal Eastern Frontier Regulation Act ka buh jingeh ia ka jylla namar ka  Bengal Eastern Frontier Regulation Act kadei ka Aiñ ba mih na ka sorkar pdeng ym dei na ka jylla, ban pynrung biang ia ka Garo Hill ki hap shna da ka bill na Parliament ym na ka state legislative assembly.
Ha kajuh ka por ka la don ka jingtynruh ba man ka por na ki wei ki sengbhalang ka jylla ba dei ban implement noh ia Meghalaya Residential Safety And Security Act (MRSSA) bad buh noh ki Entry and Exit Point.
Na ka liang ka jong ngi ngi la pynpaw la bun sien ba ka Meghalaya Residential Safety And Security Act kumba ka long mynta kam biang bad kam lah ban iada ia ka jaidbynriew, ngi pynpaw shai ruh ba ka sorkar ka dei ban pyntreikam ia ka Inner Line Permit system,  kumta ban ap ia ka Parliament ba kan amend ia ka Bengal Eastern Frontier Regulation Act kan sa shim por lane kin nym treh hi ruh lehse bad ban teinoh ia kita ki entry n exit kumba dawa kiwei ki sengbhalang kala donkam ban pynkhlain shuh shuh ia ka MRSSA 2016 bad yn pynkhlain ia ka da kaba pynrung noh ia ki kyndon jong ka Bengal Eastern Frontier Regulation Act ha ka Meghalaya Residential Safety And Security Act , lane ban pynrung ia ki kyndon jong ka inner line permit system ha ka Meghalaya Residential Safety And Security Act khnang ba kan khlain bad don ki bniat jong ka ILP.
Kita ki kyndon ki long: Ka bynta jong ka jingkhang ia ki bar jylla ban thied jaka ne khyndew la ki dei ki Tribal ne ki Non Tribal kaba don ha ka section 7 jong ka Bengal Eastern Frontier Regulation Act namar ba ka la don ka Meghalaya Land Transfer Act ka khambha ban khang noh ia ki tribal bar jylla ban thied jaka ne khyndew da kaba weng noh ia ki na ka list ha ka ST order 1950.
Kaba mut ha Meghalaya laitnoh ki Hynniewtrep bad ki Garo ki wei kim dei shuh ki Tribal bad kim lah shuh ban thied khyndew.
Ngi lah ban leh ia kane da kaba suk namar wat ka Supreme Court ruh ka la hukum ba ki immigrant kim lah ban kam ba ki dei ki ST ne SC ne OBC ha ka jylla ba ki leit poiwir.
Nalor kine, ka la idei ruh ban don ka snem ot kyrteng daba batai noh mano ki illegal resident, mano ki temporary resident bad mano ki permanent resident da kaba phah pynbeit ia ka notification kaba dei halor ka jingai Permanent Resident Certificate.
Ngi la dawa ba tang ki trai muluk (Hynniewtrep bad Garo) bad kito ki poiwir ba la sah hangne naduh u snem 1971 ki dei ban ioh ia ka Permanent Resident Certificate.
Ngi don kam ia u snem ot kyrteng namar ia ki permanent resident jong ka state ym dei ban phah shim ILP lada ki rung bad ki sah ha ka jylla, hynrei kiwei kidei ban shim.
Ngi la ai jingmut ruh ba dei ban pynkhlain bad pynbun ki kyrdop ban pyrkhing ia ki poiwir (Infiltration Check Gate) ha ka jylla ym dei ban don kita facilitation centre ban iarap bad pynsuk ia ki poiwir lyngba ki entry n exit point.
Shuh shuh ngi la dawa ba nalor ka tnad pulit (anti infiltration department) kaba ap ha ki border dei ban ai bor ia ki dorbar shong ban register ne buh jingkhein ia ki poiwir ha ki shnong, dei ban don ka hukum  ba ki poiwir kim lah ban shong shnong khlem ka jing aijingbit jong ka shnong, kaba mut nalor ka  ILP ba ioh na ka district task force dei ban ioh sa ka jingbit na ka shnong ha shwa ba ki poiwir ki shong kin sah ne kin bylla ha ka jylla.
Ki dorbar shong bad ki VDP kin don ka bor ban kem bad ujor sha ki pulit ia ki poiwir kiba rung bad sah beaiñ kadei kawei ka jingdawa kaba ngi la ban jur bha.
Ngi la pynpaw haman ki por ba ngi ia kynduh ia ka sorkar ba lada kine baroh ki kyndon kim rung  ha kata ka Jing pynkylla ia ka Meghalaya Residential Safety And Security Act ngin nym pdiang iakata ka jing pynkylla.
Balei ngi don kam ia ka ordinance namar ka Assembly kan shong dorbar satang ha u bnai August.
Ka Assam kin pyndep ka NRC ha u bnai June ne July.
Lada ka BJP ka poi biang ha ka bor ha u bnai May ki lah ban wanrah ka CAB Lyngba ka ordinance.
Lada ngi ap haduh u bnai August kamut ki dkhar na Assam da ki lakh bad ki dkhar na Bangladesh da ki klur ki la nang wan shane.
Lada ym khot special session dei ban ai  ia ka ILP lyngba ka ordinance bad sa pynlong regularise ha u bnai August namar ngi hap iada noh ia ka jaidbynriew ym long pynslem shuh.
Na ka liang ka kynhun ngi ai khublei ia baroh ki sengbhalang kiba la nang kyrshan shuh ia ka jing dawa ILP.
Ngi kyntu ia kiwei de ki sengbhalang ki bym pat kyrshan ILP ba kin sngewbha ban kyrshan lang namar lada baroh ngi dawa ILP ryngkat lang ka sorkar kan sngap bad kan pyntreikam noh kloi ia ka ILP.
Ngi kyntu ruh ia ka sorkar ba lada ka wanrah kano kano ka bill ne ka ordinance​ sngewbha da pyntip bad khot jingialang ia baroh ki sengbhalang ha ka jylla tangba dei ban khot lang ha kajuh ka por bad kajuh ka jaka iabaroh lang ym dei ban khot la ka jong ka jong  khnang ba ngin ioh ai jingmut kiba bha tam kumno yn iada ia ka jaidbynriew na ka jingma.
JOWAI : Ka tnad ka koit ka khiah jong ka West Jaiñtia Hills District kala rakhe ïaka ‘World Oral Health Day’, kaba ka phang pdeng ka dei “Say Ah! Act on Mouth Health" ha phyllaw jong ka Ummulong CHC haka sngi Balang.
La pynïaid ïa kane ka prokram da ka Dr. Rebecca Laloo Dental Surgeon NOHP, Ummulong CHC haka jingiadonlang ka kongsan ka Kong Rica Bareh CDPO, Thadlaskein Block, Dr. M Lamare Sr. Medical Officer Incharge Ummulong, ki nonghikai bad ki khynnah skul bapher bapher ka Ummulong.
Ka Dr. B. Marboh Dental Surgeon, Jowai Civil Hospital Ialong haka jingkren maitphang ka la iathuh ba ia ka World Oral Health Day la rakhe nyngkong eh haka 20 tarik Lber jong u snem 2013 halor ka thong ban pynsngewthuh ia uba bun balang halor ka koit ka khiah ki bniat bad ki bynta ba shapoh ka ktien.
Ka Dr. E. Garod Senior Dental Surgeon, Nartiang PHC kala batai pynshai shaphang ki jait jingpang ba lah ktah iaka met u briew lada ym lehkhuid ne pynkhuid bha iaki bniat khamtam haki khyllung khynnah kumjuh ki rangbah.
Naki jingpang bniat har rukom ki jingpang la ban ioh kum ka stroke, ka jingpang klongsnam, shini.
Ka ktah ruh ïaki longkmie haba armet haka kha ka pun.
Ka Dr. Garod kala ong ba dei ban pyndonkam tang 3 bnai uwei u brut kynshut bniat.
La kyntu ban lehkhuid ïaki bniat bad ka ktien ban ioh ka met kaba koit ba khiah.
Ka kongsan Kong Rica Bareh haba kren kala ong ban kiar ïa ki jingbam bym tei kum ki chips, chocolate bad kiwei kiwei ki jingbam ba thiang.
Kala kyntu ki khynnah kiban heh ban san ban bam da ki jingbam ba tei kum ki soh ki pai, ka dud ba pynbha ïaka bniat bad ruh ka koit ka khiah bad ban pynmlien ban kynshut bniat ar sien shisngi haka por mynstep bad shuwa ban thiah.
Hashwa katei ka la don ka jingiaiaid Rally ba la iashim bynta da ki khynnah skul bapher bapher ka Ummulong ban pynsngewthuh sha u paidbah halor ka jingdonkam ban ioh sumar bha ïaki bniat bad ka ktien.
La sam khusnam ruh sha ki San ngut ki khynnah kiba la ioh iaka nam Best Slogan Award ba kynthup ia u Deiwyrai Laloo na ka skul Presbyterian Ummlong, Ritreki Kharpampiah na Litter flower, Andyson Suting na Church of God, Rilem Lyngdoh na Iawpynsiñ UP bad Katdame Shylla na Lummynso UP School.
SHILLONG: U Kyrtong monlang jong ka Meghalaya Democratic Alliance (MDA) na ka United Democratic Party u Dr. Jemino Mawthoh na ka 1- Shillong Parliamentary Constituency u la ong “nga thikna ba jop ia kane ka MP Election namar ka MDA ka ieng tylli ban iakhun ia kane ka elekshon.
U Dr. Mawthoh u long u MLA barim jong ka Nongthymmai constituency bad uba long ruh u Associate Professor jong ka Centre for Adult Continuing Education (CACE) North Eastern Hills University bad u long u Chairman barim jong ka Synjuk Ki Seng Samla Shnong Central Body.
U la thep kyrteng mynta ka sngi ban iakhun pyrshah ia u MP ba mynta u Ma Vincent H Pala u kyrtong Congress.
La synran lang ia u Dr. Mawthoh da u Deputy Chief Minister ka jylla u Bah Prestone Tynsong, u ma Sniawbhalang Dhar, Samlin Malngiang, Banteidor Lyngdoh baroh lai ki myntri jong ka Sorkar MDA lem bad kiwei kiwei de.
Haba iakren bad ki lad pathai khubor, u Dr Mawthoh  ula ong ba ka jingioh vote jong ka Congress party ha ka elekshon ba dang shu dep shen haba ianujor bad ka jingioh vote jong ki seng ri lum kaba kynthup ia ka UDP, PDF, HSPDP bad ki Independents bad ka NPP ka heh haduh shiphew arphew shah ban iaka vote jong ka Congress.
U kyrtong monlang jong ka MDA u la ong ba ka long kaba bakla ban ong ba ki paidbah ki jied tang ia ki national party ha ka elekshon Lok Sabha haba u la pynkynmaw ruh ia u Prof. GG Swell (bam kwai ha Dwar U Blei) uba long na ki party ri lum bad u ba la jop ia ka elekshon MP bad udei uba tbit bad trei shitom ban iasaid n aka bynta u paidbah ha Parliament.
“Da ka jingkyrshan jong ka MDA ngan wanrah ka jingiajan hapdeng ka Sorkar Kmie bad Sorkar Jyllla kaba long kaba donkam bha," u la bynrap.
Haba kylli balei u ieng na ka UDP lada u dei u kyrtong monlang jong ka MDA, u Dr. Mawthoh u la ong ba ki paidbah ki dei ban iohi ia ka  mynsiem iatylli bad jingiatreilang jong ki dkhot jong ka MDA kiba la iawan lang kum shi iing shi sem bad kumta kampher lada ieng na kano ka party.
Ba lada u ieng na ka shap monlang ym na ka shap UDP te kala bha ba u ieng noh kum kyrtong shimet, u la bynrap.
Ka UDP ka ieng na Shillong bad ka NPP ka ieng na Tura bad ki iakhun lang ia kane ka elekshon kum ka longiing MDA, u la ong shuh shuh.
Halor ka jingkynnoh jong ka Congress ba ia ka UDP bad NPP kala shah pyniaid  haka BJP, u Dr. Mawthoh u la pynshai ba kane ka dei ka juk ka jingiatreilang bad ha ka sorkar  MDA don arngut ki MLA BJP hynrei kam mut ba ki don ka jingiadei politiks bad ka BJP.

LUMSHNONG: Ka Jaiñtia Students Movement (JSM), Eastern Region (ER) kala hiar sha ka kyrdop (Toll Gate) ka NHAI kaba don ha Lumshnong ban khang tala ïa kane ka khyrdop namar ba kala pyndik ïaka leit ka wan u paidbah naka daw ba khapngiah ka jaka.
Kane ka jingthmu ban khang tala ïaka khyrdop kala pulom, hynrei ki nongïalam ka JSM-ER hapoh ka jingïalam u Shnalad Rymbai, President bad kiwei kiwei ki dkhot ka JSM-ER kila ïoh ka lad ban ïakren bad u Executive Magistrate ka East Jaiñtia Hills District Bah Sanborn Marwein.
Kila pynsngew ha u Magistrate ba dei ban weng mardor ïa kane ka toll gate ka NHAI ha Lumshnong namar tang hapoh 50 KM ka NHAI kala buh ar tylli ki khyrdop khlem pyrkhat ïaka jingeh u paidbah ka East bad West Jaiñtia.
“Ka NHAI kala leh bor shaba palat ha kaba tang hapoh 50 KM ka jingngai kala buh ar tylli ki khyrdop khlem pyrkhat ïa u paidbah nalor ba suki ka rukom pynïaid ïa kine ki khyrdop khrong pisa", la ong u Shnalad Rymbai.
Ula bynrap ba ki paidbah ka East Jaiñtia haduh mynta ym pat lah ban siew dep ïaka bai musur khyndew naka bynta ban shna ïaka surok.
Ka JSM-ER kala dawa naka NHAI ban shna pyndep ïaki nala ne ki nur ki jaka iaid kjat (footpath) ban shngain kai aid ka ieng u paidbah.
U Executive Magistrate ula kular shimkhia ban pynsngew sha u DC East Jaiñtia Hills halor ka jingdawa ka JSM ER bad la pynbeit ban ïakren lashai ka sngi halor ka toll gate ha Rilum Jaiñtia bad ka JSM-ER kala byrthen ba lada ym ïoh iaki jingdawa kan ïakhih da kaba tyngeh.

LUMSHNONG : “Ha kine ki sngi baroh u briew, tang ban pynsngewbha ïaki para briew, ula ïakyrsum lang haka bymdei lane leh bakla lang kaba buh ïalade haka jingma," ong u Pastor GPL Gadew.
“Mynta lada phai sha ka shynshar khadar, haka shakri sorkar, haka imlang sahlang naduh na ïing haduh sha bar kam don shuh ka jingshisha ne ka hok.
Hynrei baroh ngi la pyndem haka bymdei bad ïa kyrsumlang, ïa mynjurlang ban leh ïa kaei kaei ka bym dei", la ong u Pastor Gadew haba kren haka Jingiaseng KJP Synod Mihngi kaba 17 ha Balang Presbyterian Lumshnong kaba hap haka Narpuh District, Narpuh Border Presbytery.
Kane ka jingïaseng kala sdang haka 14 tarik Lber bad kala poi sha kaba kut haka Sngi U Blei.
Ka matpdeng jong kane ka jingïaseng kadei “To sharai, to ieng skhem ha ka jingngeit" (1 Kor. 16:13).
U Pastor Gadew haba sam ïaka khubor naka ktien U Blei ha kane ka jingïaseng synod haka por 1:30 baje nohphaisngi, ula sot na ka Shithi u Apostol Paul sha ki nong Galatia 1:10 – “Namar hato mynta nga bhoh ïaki briew, ne ïa U Blei? Lane nga wad ïa kaban pynsngewbha ïaki briew? Lada nga dang pynsngewbha ïaki briew, ngam shym long u shakri U Khrist".
U Pastor Gadew ula ong ba u briew mynta ula wad tang ban pynsngewbha para briew ban ïoh bynta ban sngewbhalang bad u la pyndem ha kaei kaei ka bym dei.
Bad ula ong ba “Ka pop mynta kala trei bor bah haka jingim u briew bad ula pyndem haka pyrthei bad klet ïa ka jingshisha".
Ka pop pyndem bym dei kala ktah ha manla uwei pa ka wei, bunsien ka jia haka jingshongkha kiba ïapher niam kaba jur ka iatan tyllai sha kano ka niam ban pynskhem bad barabor ka la jop ka spah.
Ka juh ka jia ha ki kmie ki kpa ki pyndem ha khmat ki khun bad pynbiang ïaka jingdawa jong ki.
Ula ai nuksa ïaka jingjied nongmihkhmat haba u nongialeh ne u kyrtong u pynbam pisa; ki paidbah ki ïa kmen ïaka pisa bad pyndem ïalade bad bam ïaka pisa bad dei tad dor ïalade.
Ha khaii pateng u Khristan ruh u tuh u thok bad ïakyrsumlang haka ahor ka pop bad ka pyrthei ban bamsap bamklop ban ïoh pynsngewbha ïalade.
Haka jingiaseng 10:30 Am, U Pastor RH Lyngkhoi ula sam ïaka khubor U Blei kaba ula sot naka Kitab U Joel 2:13.
U Pastor ula khot ïaki para bangeit ka balang Presbyterian ban kylla kaba mut bad ban nym pynsyriem ïalade bad ka pyrthei bad nym ïaleh pyrshah bad ka hukum U Trai.
Ka Synod kaba 18 kan long ha Balang Presbyterian Dkhiah West, East Jaiñtia Hills District.
JOWAI: Ki shipai ïada khappud India Bangladesh- ki Border Security Force (BSF) jong ka Hawaitilla bad ka Jaliakhola BOP kila ïoh kurup haduh 61 tylli masi dab ba shongdor duna T. 13 lak ba thmu ban khaïi tuh sha Bangladesh lyngba kitei ki shnong, kiba don ha khappud India-Bangladesh.
Ki shipai BSF kila ïoh kurup ïa kine 61 tylli ki masi dab tang haki 3 sngi.
Haka 12 tarik Lber ki shipai BSF kila ïoh kurup 32 tylli ki masi dab kiba shong T. 6,84,800/- na Jaliakhola.
Haka 15 tarik Lber la ioh kurup 3 tylli ki Masi ba shongdor T. 64,200/- na Hawaitilla BOP.
Haka 17 tarik Lber la ïoh kurup biang sa 26 tylli ki masi  na Hawaitilla BOP kiba shongdor T. 5,45,600/-.
La ioh kurup ia kine ki masi haka por mynmiet bad shiteng synia bad ki shipai kim shym la ïohkem ïano iano ruh kiba donkti ban shalan tuh ia kine ki masi namar ka jingrben ka khlaw bad ka jingdum.
Ki shipai kila aiti iaki masi sha ki pulit bad ujor ruh ïaka ejahar.
La iathuh baka ki masi kila tlot naka jingshah sympat lathi bad jingbym biang ka bam.
Ki Shipai kila ujor ka ejahar ha Muktapur Police Patrol Post ha kaba kila dep ban register case katkum ka kyndon aiñ ba lehbeiñ iaki mrad mreng.

JOWAI: Ka Jingïaseng Samla kaba 17 jong ka KJP Synod Mihngi kan long ha Balang Wapungskur, East Jaiñtia Hills.
Kane ka jingiaseng kan sdang naduh ka sngi Thohdieng bad ki dkhot ka Balang baroh ki la dep ban pynkhreh nadong shadong ban pdiang ïa kane ka jingïaseng kaba heh jong ka Balang Presbyterian.
Ka khubor kaba la ïoh na u Pastor T Dkhar, uba dei u Pastor In charge ka Balang Wapung, u la ïathuh ba kane ka jingïaseng samla ka KJP Synod Mihngi kan kut ha ka sngi U Blei bad ha kane ka sngi, ki nongïathuh khana lane nongkren ba kyrpang ki long u Pastor BD Shangdiar u ban ai ka jingkren ha ka jingïaseng paidbah haka por 10:00 mynstep bad u Pastor SG Ryngksai ha ka jingïaseng nohphai sngi kaba 1:30 pm katba u Pastor EL Kharmawphlang pat un ai ka jingkren halor ka subject ba la buh ha ka jingiaseng por 6:30pm.
Na ka liang ka Balang ka la mana ïa kino kino ki ba wan die jingbam sha katei ka jaka.
Ha kajuh ka por ka Balang ka khot ka wer ia baroh ki para ba ngeit na kiba lang bapher bapher bad kiba na kiwei pat ki Balang sha katei ka jingïaseng ba kin ioh ka jingkyrkhu na u Trai.
Ka kam ki paidbah kala kut bad mynta ka lah poi sa ka pali ki rangbah ia kiba ngi la pynkup ia ka bor bad iktiar kum ki MDC, ha KHADC bad JHADC jongngi, ban ai ia u synniang shakri sha ka Jaitbynriew Hynniewtrep lyngba ki ADC.
Hangne harum, nga kwah ban kdew ia ki katto katne ki mat ia kiba ki ar tylli ki Distrik Konsil ki dei ban shimkhia ban pyntreikam ha kine ki san snem kiban wan:-  Ka Jinglong Laitluid ki Distrik Konsil: Ban iakhun pynurlong ia ka Bor treikam laitluid (Autonomy) jong ki Distrik Konsil khlem kano kano ka jingtuklar na ki tnat sorkar kum ka District Council Affairs (DCA) ka Sorkar Jylla bad ka Ministry of Home Affairs(MHA) ka Sorkar Pdeng kan long ka thong kaba hakhmat duh jong ki MDC thymmai jongngi.
Ngi la iohi ia ka jingsahkut jong kiba bun bah ki Bill ba la pass da ki ADC, ki bym shym la ioh iaka Assent jong u Governor ka jylla.
La khein iaki ADC tang kum i shnat rit (Sub- Department) jong ka DCA.
La khein khiew jakai ia ka rai ki nongmihkhmat ba la jied da u paidbah trai ri ban shna ain kanun na ka bynta ka biang ka shngain bad ka skhem jongki hala muluk hala Ri.
Ha kane ka rukom ba mynta, u Ophisar ne wat u LDA ka DCA u kham khraw ban iaki 120 ngut ki MDC ka KHADC, JHADC bad GHADC, ban ia ka Sixth Schedule bad ban ia ki paidbah kiba la jied iakiha ki elekshon iajied MDC.
Ym tang katta, hynrei ha ki bnai bad snem bala leit noh, ngi sakhi ba wat ka MHA jong ka Sorkar Kmie ruh ka la wan tuklaria ki Bill Jong ki ADC bad ia kane la pynshisha lyngba ka ishu VAB.
Ka por bad ka kam ka dawa, namarkata iaki MDC ban iakhun dohiap halor kane ka phang khnang ba kan ym iai long ka jingibein ia ka mon jongngi u paidbah ne ia ka iktiar ki ADC kum ki shlem thaw ain ia kiba la pynkupbor da ka Riti Synshar ka Ri India lyngba ka Sixth Schedule.
Ka Jingpynkylla ia ka Sixth Schedule: Ka por ka dawa iaki MDC baroh ban iathir sani halor kumno ban wanrah ia ka jingpynkylla ha ka Sixth Schedule ka Riti Synshar ka Ri India, namar la i donkam kyrkieh ban pynbha bad pynkhlain shuhshuh ia ka Sixth Schedule Amendment Bill kaba lah poi ha Rajya Sabha  ka Parliament ka Ri India.
Kane ka Bill ka don shibun bah ki jingdkoh ki ban wanrah jingma iangi ki trai ri riewlum ritpaid ka Ri.
Kawei na kita ka long halor ka jingioh MDC ka GHADChaduh 42 ngut katba ka KHADC pat ka ioh tang 40 ngut; ka jingpynbeit ka long kaba noh shiliang tarajur, namar ha ki pud ka KHADC ki don haduh 29 ngut ki MLA katba ha ki pud ka GHADC, ki don tang 24 ngut kumba ka long mynta.
Sa kawei pat ka jingduna ka long halor ka kyndon ban buh MDC shu sieh da kiwei pat ki riewlum ki bym dei ki Khasi, Jaintia bad Garo.
Lada longkam kane, ngam tip ngin dang lah ne em ban pakhang ia ki bym dei ki riewlum ban thep vote ha ki elekshon ADC.
Kumno ruh ka lah ban long ba ka Sorkar jylla kan rai ban pynduh syndon ia ki Dorbar Shnong bad ban bujli pynban ha ka jaka jongki da ki Village Council bad Municipal Council.
Kane hawto kam dei ka jingtuklar ia u pudtreikam ki Distrik Konsil? Hynrei, don ruh ki bynta ka Amendment Bill ia kiba ngi dei ban kyrshan, bad kita ki long, halor ka Ain Kyntiap Seng ( Anti- Defection) ia ki MDC bad ruh de, halorka Direct Funding.
Ia ka Para 3 jong ka Amendment Bill ruh donkam ban pynbeit namar ba ki ADC ki donkam ban ioh bor shuh shuh khamtam ha kaba iadei bad ka khyndew ka shyiap, ki khlaw ki btap, ka jingiada na ka jingrung laitlan ki mynder ri bad kiwei de.
Dei ban pynkylla ruh ia ka Para12 A (a) bad (b) khnang ban aibor pura ia ki Distrik Konsil bad kumjuh ka Para 20 khnang ban ioh pynbeit noh ia u pud u sam.
Ki Dorbar Trai Ri bad ka iktiar jongki: La i donkam kyrkieh ban ithuh bad ban pynkupbor ia ki Dorbar Trai Ri kum ki Dorbar Shnong, Dorbar Kur, Dorbar Raid, Dorbar Hima bad kumta terter.
Ia ki ain jong ki Hima dei ban kham pynkhlain shuhshuh; bad naka bynta ki Hima ki bym pat don jingthoh ain, dei ban shna noh mardor.
Ki MDC ka KHADC ki dei ban buddien halor ka Clan Administration Bill bad ban pynthikna ban pynioh shen ia ka jingmynjur u Lat ka jylla, iaka.
Ka JHADC ruh kadei ban sdang thaw ain noh halor kane ka bynta.
Ka Kam Khaii Pateng: Dei ban pynkhlain shuh shuh ia ka Trading by Non-tribal Act bad kumjuh ki rules jongka.
Ka khaii pateng kaba long u budlum bad u syngkai ka ioh ka kot ka dei ban wanphai biang sha ka kti ki trai ri trai muluk bad ia ka kam khaii Benami dei ban pynduhjait syndon.
Halor ki Ain Iada Riti: Ia ki ain iada Riti bad iada dustur kum ka Lineage Bill la donkam ban pynioh iaka jingmynjur jong u Lat ka jylla.
Kum shibynta ban ai mynsiem ia ki rangsamla jongngi ba kin sngewskhem ha ka kolshor jongngi, lah ban wanrah ruh ia ki ain kum ka Inheritance Bill , ha kaba ki shynrang ruh kin ioh bynta lang na ka spah , ki jingdon jingem bad ka kam ka khaii jong ki kmie ki kpa kum ba long ki khun kynthei.
Halor ka Synshar Sor: Ia ka rukom synshar sor (town administration )dei ban pynbeit noh hapdeng ki ADCbad ka Sorkar Jylla khnang ban weng noh ia ka jingkyntur pud kaMUDA, bad kumjuh ban lait na ka jingiatyngkhuh ki ain shna iing ka MUDA bad jong ki ADC.
Ka Independent Ilaka Tribunal: Ka Synshar khadar trai ri, ha baroh ki kyrdan ka dei ban lait na ka kam iakhleh jaktung politiks.
Lyngba ka jingsdang ia ka Independent Ilaka Tribunal, ka ban shimbishar halor kino kino ki kam buaid politics da ki bor synshar trai ri kum ki Dorbar Shnong, Dorbar Raid bad kiwei de ki khlieh nongsynshar.
Halor ki kam pynroi: La donkam kyrkieh ban wanrah ia ka District Council Development Advisory Board ka ban ai jingmut halor kumno ban wanrah ia ki kam pynroi ha ki jaka u pud u sam ki Distrik Konsil.
Ka Kam Khajna: Ka jingiatyngkhuh bad ka Sorkar Jylla halor ka Royalty na ki mar pohkhyndew ne ki dieng ki siej ka la ju wanrah jingeh bun bun sien ia ki ADC.
Donkam ban pynbeit pynjanai ia ka rukom lum khajna lum musur ki ADC khnang ban pynthikna ba ka thiartyngka ki ADC kan dap naka bynta ki kam kiba bun kiba ki dei ban leh bad pyndep.
Ka Khuid ka Suba ha ka kam pisa tyngka : La i donkam kyrkieh ban wanrah ia ka rukom treikam kaba khuid ba suba ha KHADC bad JHADC jongngi.
Ka kolshor thungkam sopsop ka dei ban duh noh; ka kam lum khajna lum musur ka dei ban long kaba khuid, ba ryntih bad ka bym don kano kano ka kam bamtuh ne bamsap.
Halor ka Ktien, ka Kolshor bad ka Rwai ka Shad bad kiwei de ki Sap Bad jingstad tynrai trai ri: Kum ki nongda nongri ia ka lariti ba kyrpang bad riewspah jongngi, kan dei ka kamram jong ki Distrik Konsil ban lumthup ha ki jingthoh ne ki phlim ne ki dur ia ki drama, ki khana puriskam, ki jingshad jingrwai tynrai na kylleng ka bri u Hynniewtrep.
Kumjuh de, halor ka sap trai ri ha ka liang ka sumar pang lyngba ka khem ka spud bad kumjuh ki kynbat dawai; ia kane ruh dei ban buhbeit lyngba ki kot ne ki dur ne ki phlim khnang ba ka pyrthei salonsar kan iohi ia ka jingmaian jong ka jingshemphang bad jingstad ia kaba la ai pateng hangi da ki kni ki kpa myndai.
Kine ka sienjam, ki long shibynta na ka jingpyrshang ban buhbeit, ban pynneh pynsah bad ban pynpaw de sha ka pyrthei ia ka jingriewspah bad jingkyrpang ka ktien, ka kolshor bad ka rukom im jongngi.
Namar kata, ka jingkhot ka long shaphi ki MDC ia kiba ngi la pynkhamti ia ka bor ka iktiar ban ialam iangi; ba phin long u Sangot jong ka jingangnud jongngi, u Khulom jong ka jingthrang jong ka Jaitbynriew Hynniewtrep Hynniewskum ban pynneh pynsah, ban kyntiew bad ban kyrsiew iala ka jait ka khong bad ban iada iaka na ki ‘phliah ding ba pynbijai’ ka pyrthei shai.
Ngi la pynsleh iaphi , wat pynlehrain iangi, bad kumjuh ialade bad iaki kular ba phi la khlei hakhmat u briew u Blei ban shakri khlem manthait iala ka Jaitbynriew lyngba ka rynsan ki ADC.
Da u Bah Robertjune Kharjahrin.

U Pastor BB Lamin ula pynïaid ïaka jingïalang bad ka Headmistress Jowai District Presbyterian School (JDPS) ka Kong R Bamon kala ïathuh ïaka history lyngkot ka skul.

JOWAI : Ka Lakroh Mini Hydel Project kaba la sdang ban sorjamin bad tohkit bniah ban pynmih bording naduh u snem 1990, kala urlong  bad la plie paidbah ïaka haka sngi ba ar da u MLA ka War Jaiñtia bad u Myntri ka tnad Pule Puthi u Ma Lahkmen Rymbui.
Ha kane ka jingplie paidbah la ïadonlang u Deputy Commissioner, West Jaiñtia Hills u Ma Garod LSN Dykes, u SP West Jaiñtia Hills u Bah Lakador Syiem nalor ki engineer MeECL, MPGCL bad u paidbah nongshong shnong ka khappud India Bangladesh.
Kane ka projek bording Lakroh Mini Hydel Project la sdang ïaka jingjurip jaka bad tohkit naduh u snem 1990 da kaba MeSEB kaba tip mynta kum ka MeECL.
Ha u Lber 20, 1990 u Lat barim ka Jylla u A. A. Rahim haba kren haka ïing dorbar ka Jylla ula ong, “Ka jingtohkit iaka jingtrei naka bynta ka  Lakroh Micro Hydel Project la lah ban pyndep.
Kane ka projek lada lah ban pyndep kan pynmyntoi ïaki shnong ha thain nongkyndong.
Bad dei mynta u Lber 05, 2019 la lah ban plie paidbah ïaka ba kan pynbiang bording ïaki 14 tylli ki shnong ha Elaka Satpator ba hap ha khappud India Bangladesh.
Kane ka jaka pynmih bording ka MPGCL ka dei kaba shongdor T. 21. 43 Klur.
La bei pisa naka Ministry of New and renewable Energy, Government of India (MNRE) T. 6. 75 klur bad ka North Eastern Council (NEC) T. 5 Klur kaba duna la hap ban buria da ka tnad T. 9.68 klur, la ong u Director (Generation) MePDGCL Bah K Tiewsoh.
Kane ka projek pynmih bording dei kaba tip kum ka ‘Run of the River’ ne kaba ym don kam jaka pyllang um hynrei la shu den iaka um ban sam sha ka Power House.
Ka don haka bynta ka wah Lakroh, hajan ka shnong Muktapur, West Jaiñtia Hills Disrtict bad ka jngai 6 KM na Muktapur.
Ha u snem 2001 jong u bnai Lber la mang pisa haka dor 11.76 core da ka MNRE bad MNRE kala ïarap pisa T.6.75 Core bad ka NEC T.5 core.
Namar ka jingrem ki kor ki bor ym shym la lah satia ban buh ar tylli ki machine ma 750 KW, ka sorkar pdeng kala bthah ia ka MeECL ban buh noh tang kawei ka machine ban pynmih bording 1500 KW bad kane la rai ha u snem 2003", la ong shuh shuh u Bah Tiewsoh.
La shna iaka jaka pyllang um haka 40 meter ka lynter bad ka jingjrong ne ka jylliew kala kot 4.5 meter kaba lah ban pynlang iaka um 1150 litre ka um shi second.
Na ka jaka tan um sha ka nala ba 800 meter ka um kan leit sha ka kynja pyllang um (forebay) ba lah ban pyndap 4 lak 50 hajar litre bad sam sha ka power house.
Ka um kaba mih naka power house la phah sha ki hali ki pynthor (kaba tip kum ka tail race) ban pynbiang iaka um sha ki hali ki pynthor ban rep ban riang.
Hadien kane ka projek sam bording kala sahkut namar ka jingbym ioh NOC bad jaka shna power house bad la sdang iaka jingtrei naduh u snem 2009.
La mang ban pyndep iaka projek ha u snem 2013, hynrei ki tiar kiba la thied ki don katto katne kiba sniew, hynrei ka MeSEB (MeECL) ka kyrduh pisa bad ym lah satia ban pyndep ïaka projek wat hadien bala dep ban pyllut 11 Klur eiei, iathuh u bah Tiewsoh.
Shuwa ban kut u snem 2017 la thied iaki tiar tar bad ha u November 2017 la lah ban pyndep bad la pyndait ïaki kor ki bor bad la lah ban pynmih bording.
Baroh ka jinglut jingsep kala kot T.21 43 bad buria ka MePGCL 9.68 Klur.
U Bah K Tiewsoh ula ong ba ka dor pynmih bording kane ka hydel projek ka long tang T.1 tyngka 58 naia.
Kane ka projek ka dei ban pyndep hapoh lai snem, hynrei la lah ban pyndep hadein 18 snem naduh u snem 2001, la ong u bah K Tiewsoh.
“Lyngba kane ka projek kan ïarap iaka jylla ha kaban kyntiew iaka pynmih bording naka 354.7 MW sha 356.2 MW bad tang kane ka projek kan injek ne ai ding 11 million unit haka shisnem," la ong u Bah Tiewsoh.
U Ma Lahkmen Rymbui haba kren kum u kongsan ula ong “Ka MeECL kam duna shuh shuh haka jingtip jingshemphang ban maitphang ne trei kum kine ki projek, hynrei haba shna kino kino ki projek dei ban pyndep haka por kaba biang lait shah ktah na ka jingkiew dor ki mar ki mata bad ban lait na jingsahkut ka jingtrei iaki skim ne projek".

Na Thomas Jones la shah ban iaid kali bad ba kin mih sha Dulong College Road.

Ki kali jong ki Zonal and Sector Officers (Civil and Policela shah ban iaid lyngba ka Wah Nangbah haduh DC bad ïaki kali yn pynieng ha Nongbah Stand.

Naka liang u nongialam ka seng u samla Richard Mawkhiew ula ong ba kane ka jingot tulop kadei ka jingiuh roit bad ka jingbymkhein snep iaki trai ri ki trai Muluk.

JOWAI: Ha man ki Sengniam, Sengkur, Seng Hima Sima, ki Dorbar shnong, ne wat haka kynhun shipai ruh u don beit u Nongialam u ban ialam iaka kynhun laka long ha kano kano ka bynta kaba ia tyngkhuh.
Khlem u nongialam ngim juh poi shaei shaei ruh bad ngim lah leh eiei ruh khlem u nongialam.
Kumta ban lah ban  pyniaid beit iaka kam shakhmat ngi donkam ban jied ia u Nongialam.
Ha baroh kitei ki bynta, ngi donkam ban ioh ia ki nongialam kiba stad bad kiba shemphang ban pyniaid beit ia ka kam.
Ki nongialam ki dei ban long ki briew kiba don ka jinglah ym tang ha ka thoh ka tar hynrei ha ka kren ka khana bad ha ka kam kaba iadei bad ki paidbah, ne ki ophis ba iadonbynta lang.
Ka jingdon ka kyrdan pule kaba biang ka iarap shibun eh ban long ki nongialam hynrei ka sap kaba shong tynrai ha u ne ka ki long ki bynta ka jingkyrkhu U Blei.
Kito kiba la don lypa ia ka kyrdan pule kaba biang ki lah ban hikai da kaba suk ia ki jingdonkam bad ki kyndon kumno ban long ki nongialam.
Baroh ki don la ka jong ka jong ka sap bad kam dei eh tang ha ka kam trei paidbah hynrei wat ha la i jong i rympei iing ruh donkam ban don ki nongialam.
U Nongialam udei ban long uba lah ban pyniajan bad pyniadei bad u paidbah (Public Relation) khnang ba yn lah ban pyniaid beit iaka kam ka jam sha khmat.
U nongialam udei ba long pdeng (neutral) khlem da don ka mynsiem niew shilliang khmat ne sngewiapher Niam.
Udei ban long uba kloi ban pdiang iakino kino ki jingshah kren ne shah kynthoh namar haba long nongialam kin mih beit ki jingshah kynthoh.
Ban jop ia kano kano ka mat kaba iakhun U Nongialam udei ban long uba tbit  ban ialam iaka kynhun laka long directly ne indirectly.
U nongialam u dei ban don ka sap ban pyndonkam iaka buit, ne ka jabieng ban jop iaka issue.
U Nongialam u dei ruh ban don ka sap ban kren hakata ka rukom khnang ban lah ban pynhun, pynkohnguh ia ki nongbud bad ruh ban pynsngewthuh iaki ba ia tyngkhuh kam.
Kumta haba ngi jied ia u nongialam ngi dei ban long kiba stad ban jied.
Haba ong stad ban jied kam mut ba ngi hap ban pass iaki kyrdan ba heh, hynrei ngi dei ba peit ia u Nongialam u bastad uba shemphang bad u batbit.
Ngim dei ban jied ia u briew tang namar ba ngi lah ioh bai sha  na u , ngim dei ban jied ia u briew tang namar ba u Bun Spah Bun Phew, Ngim dei ban jied ia u briew tang namar ba u dei uba ia jan.
Shibun kiei kiei kiba donkam iangi ban bishar bniah bha bin pa bin hashwa ba ngin jied ia u nongialam.
Namar lada bakla ban jied ia u nongialam kan don ka jingeh kaba khraw tam hadien ha bud.
Kumta haba ngi jied ia u nongialam ngi dei ban pyrkhat janai bad puson bha ymdei ban shu jied mata madei kat ia uba lap ne kat ia uba kloi ban ai baisha namar ka ban long nongialam kamdei ka kam kaba suk.
Ka 5 snem kadei ka kaba kordor tam haka synshar paidbah.
Ban thaw iakino ki ki ain kiba iada ia ka jaitbynriew ngi donkam ia u nongialam uba stad bad u ba shem.
Kaba khadduh tam ka dei ban jied da ki Nongialam kiba lah tbit( experienced) namar kim donkam shuh ban dang hap batai ne hap pan jingiarap na kiwei pat haba ki mut leh eiei.
Hynrei ki shu leh hi ia ka ei kaba ki thmu ban leh namar ki lah don lypa ka jingshemphang na lade.
Da U Ma Nangai Sutnga.

Ka Sorkar pdeng dang shen kala mynjur ïaka jingpynkylla thymmai (Amendment) ïa ka Sixth Schedule bad kane kan iarap ïaka konsil ban khia ka pla tyngka, hynrei ka donkam pat ïaki nongmihkhmat kiba trei shitom kumnoi ban pynpoi ïaki kam pynroi sha u paidbah, la ong u Ma Moonlight Pariat.
Ula ong ïaki paidbah ba kim dei ban shah pynbieij haka tyngka pliah ka NPP, namar ba ki briew kiba don haka NPP kila kylla long kiba lalot bad ki ba khwan myntoi shimet.
“Wat khih paloh ki jingmut jingpyrkhat jong phi haka tyngka pliah ba shisngi namar ba kane ka pisa ka dei tang ban khring ïaka vote jong phi, marsien jop baroh ka pisa kan leit sha ka pla jong ki", ula ong u Ma Pariat.

JOWAI: Ki ba bun ki Dorbar Shnong ha rilum Jaiñtia kila dep shim rai lypa ïano ban vote haka elekshon bad kane ka pyndiaw ïa kiba bun ki samla ki ban thep ïaka vote kaba nyngkong ka jong ki haka MDC election.
Ka kynhun jong ki samla pule kila pynpaw ka jingsngewkhia halor ka jinglong jingman ha Ri Lum Jaiñtia namar ba ki Dorbar Shnong kila khleh politik.
Ki Dorbar Shnong jong ki katto katne ki shnong kila dep shim rai lypa ban jied ïa u kyrtong monlang uba la pynieng da ka shnong  bad ki nongshong shnong ruh kin kyrshan ïa uta u kyrtong ba ka kyrshan.
Haba kylli balei ba kim pyrshah ïaka rai jong ki Dorbar Shnong, ki katto katne ki samla pule (bym kwah pynpaw kyrteng) ki la ong ba katto katne ki nongïalam jong ka Dorbar Shnong hadien ba kila dep ïasyllok para ma ki bad ki shim rai ïa uno u nongshong shnong ne kyrtong ban jied kum u kyrtong monlang bad hadien kata kin sa pynlong ia ka Dorbar ba kumno re kumno ki pynrung ha ka khlieh ki nongshong shnong bad jied ia uta kum u kyrtong monlang.
Uwei na ki samla pule u la ong ba ka Constitution jong ka Ri India ka la pynkup bor ia ki nongshong shnong ïa ka hok ban kren laitluid bad pyrkhat ne leh laitluid ne kata ka freedom of speech and expression kaba mut u ne u ki don hok ban jied laitluid ïano ïano ha ka elekshon.
Hynrei kane ka jingjied kyrtong monlang da ka Dorbar Shnong kala iuhroit noh ïa ka hok jong ki nongshong shnong ban jied laitluid ïaki nongmihkhmat.
Kane ka rai jong ka Dorbar shnong kala wanrah ka jingbym sngewtynnad ïa kiba bun ki samla kiba dang shu ïoh vote thymmai bad lada ki mut ban leh pyrshah ruh ka wanrah ka jingshah tharai sniew na ki nongïalam shnong bad bun ki sheptieng ban ïaid pyrshah ïaka shnong namar ïoh jia ba shah kyntait haka imlang ka sahlang ne ka shah tait shnong.
Kine ki samla pule kila pynpaw ïaka jingbynniaw ba ka aiñ pynkup bor ïaki Waheh Shnong-Ka Jaintia Hills Autonomous District (Establishment of Elaka and Village and Election, Appointment, Powers, Functions and Sirdars of Dolloi/Sirdar and Waheh Shnong) Act 2015 namar ba kam shym la kdew shai ne khang ïa ki Dorbar Shnong khamtam u Waheh Shnong (katkum ka Sanad) ban ïasylla haki kam politik ne elekshon bad dei kane kaba ki pynmih ïaki rai kiba pyrshah ïaka hok jong u nongshong shnong.
“Ki don katto katne ki Dorbar Shnong kila dep rai jied nongmihkhmat bad la maham ruh ban pynduh ïaki jingiarap ia ki briew ba ialeh pyrshah ia ka rai ka Dorbar Shnong", la ong kawei ka longkmie kaba hapoh Jowai constituency.
Kaba phylla ba ka bor pynïaid elekshon haka Jylla ne ka District ki ialap ban pynlong ïaka jingthep vote kaba khuid kaba suba, hynrei kumba jia long ha Rilum Jaiñtia bun hi ki Dorbar Shnong ki ïasylla politik bad la dep pynbna sha ki lad pathai khubor ba rai kyrshan ïa u/ka kyrtong ha ki dorbar shnong bad ki bor pynïaid District ki leh kuman.
Mynta kine ki samla pule ki phai khmat tang sha ka ïing bishar High Court ban kan tuklar bad tehlakam ïaki Dorbar Shnong bad khang pyrshah ïaki shnong na ki kam elekshon bad ban jied kyrtong monlang.

SHILLONG: Ki dkhot ka Khasi Students Union (KSU) ha ryngkat ki sharak dongmusa bad ka jingpynbthei ïa ki bom pataka, kila pdiang burom ïa ki nongialam ka KSU bad ia u Chairman ka North East Students’ Organization (NESO) u Bah Samuel Jyrwa haka miet sngi Palei ha Jaiaw, Madan Weiking, Shillong halor ka jingjop ban pynpulom ïaka jingthmu wanrah ïaka CAB ha Rajya Sabha.
Une nongialam ka NESO bad kiwei kiwei kila her sha nongbah Delhi haka taiew bala dep ban kyrpad ïaki nongïalam ki seng saiñ hima bapher ban pyrshah ïaka CAB ha Rajya Sabha, kaba la pynpulom noh ka jingthmu wanrah ïaka CAB haka Rajya Sabha bad kala iap artad.
Ha kane jingpdiang burom la ïadonlang ki sengbhalang ba kynthup ia ka SSSS, FKJGP, TULBA, Shillong Assamese Social Cultural Student Association (SASCSA) bad kiwei kiwei.
Shuwa kane la pdiang burom ruh ïa u Bah Samuel Jyrwa Chairman ka NESO bad ki dkhot sengbhalang ha Guwahati airport da ki nongialam ka NESO.
U Bah Samuel Jyrwa ula ong ba “ka sorkar India ka thmu ban thombor ïa ngi la 50-60 snem mynshuwa bad mynta ka jingthmu ka long ban thombor sa da ki paidbah na Bangladesh ban pynkylla madan lut ia ka ri ka jong ngi bad ia ka thain Shatei Lammihngi hi baroh kawei."
U la khublei ruh ba da ka jingtrei shitom bad ka jingïatylli jong ki sengbhalang ha ka thain Shatei Lammihngi kaba la lah pynpulom iaka jingthmu pynlong aiñ ka CAB. Naduh 2016, ka NESO kala ieng pyrshah iaka CAB, hyrnei ka sorkar India kam patiaw bad ha kane ka kynti da ka jingmih u paidbah bad ki sengbhalang bapher naduh Khasi Students’ Union (KSU), ka All Assam Students’ Union (AASU), ka Naga Students Federation (NSF), ka Mizo Zirlai Pawl (MZP), ka Twipra Students’ Federation (TSF), ka All Manipur Students’ Union (AMSU), ka Garo Students’ Union (GSU) bad ka All Arunachal Pradesh Students’ Union (AAPSU) kala pynurlong ïaka jingdawa.

SHILLONG: Ka School of Classical Guitar, hapoh ka jing kyrshan jong ka Music in Home ryngkat ka jingiatreilang jong ka Indian Guitar Federation bad ka Big FM 98.3 Shillong, kan pynlong ia ka Concert ha ki sur jong ka Guitar kaba lah ai kyrteng ia ka kum “Ka Janmiet Ha Ki Sur Jong Ka Classical Guitar".
Ha kane ka Concert kin don arngut ki nongtem guitar kiba bna nam jong ka pyrthei kata U Matt Bacon na USA bad U Padet Netpakdee na Thailand.
Khyndiat shaphang U Matt Bacon, ha jingiaid lynti jong U ha ka liang jong ka put ka tem, U Matt Bacon U la long teng U nongjop ha ka “Texas National Music Festival" “Classical Mind" ha kajuh ka por U long ruh U Nongthoh Jingrwai, U recording artists, bad U nonghikai ha kawei napdeng ki skul ha ka put ka tem jong U A. R. Rahman ka KM Conservatory of Music kaba don ha Chennai India.
U Matt Bacon U la iohpdiang ia ka Master degree na San Fancrisco Conservatory of Music ha U snem 2014 bad ia ka B.A na Peaboy Institute of John Hopkins University ha U snem 2010.
Ha baroh ar ki kyrdan U Matt u la wan shakhmat bad U la ioh ia ka merit scholarship, bad ka khusnam da ka Carrier Development Grants.
Halor U Padet, la kha ia U ha Chiang Mai, Thailand bad U la sdang ia ka put kam tem lyngba ki tiar put tiar tem tynrai jong ka Ri Thailand.
U la ioh ia ka Gold Medal Price haba U dang don tang 14 snem karta ha ka jingiakop tem guitar ha ka Thailand kaba la tip kim ka Thailand Youth Music Competition lyngba jong kane ka khusnam ka la pynlong ban shim ia ka rai ban pynlong ia ka put ka tem kum ka kam ha ka jingim ka jong U.
Kane ka long kum kaba sdang napdeng ki jingjop ki jong U ha ka put ka tem kaba kynthup ia ka 1st prize na la Thailand International Guitar Competition 2019.
U Padet U la ioh ia ka jinghikai ha ka guitar na ki nongtem Classical Guitar kiba paw jong ka Pyrthei kiba kynthup ia Leon Kaudelak, Sergio Asad bad David Tanenbaum.
Nalor ba U la long U nongtem Clasdical Guitar uba la ih bha, U ju pynlut por ruh ialade ban pynbeit sur na kiwei ki jait jingtem sha ka Guitar bad U ju thaw ruh ia ki sur ha ka Guitar bad kiwei de.
Da ka jingthmu ban pynsaphriang bad ban kyntiew ia ka jingtem ha ka Classical Guitar, La seng ia ka School of Classical Guitar ha U snem 2016.
Naduh ba la seng ia ka, kum ka Skul ka la pynlong ia shibun ki guitar concert bad ki guitar workshop nalor ka jing ai jinghikai sha ki khynnah ha ka theory bad ka practical ruh kumjuh kaba iadei bad ka western classical music bad ban ka skul ka pynialeh examin ruh ia ki khynnah ha ki grade exam na ki international music board kiba pher jong ka pyrthei.
Khnang ba kan long ka Concert kaba jop bad ka kaban pynhun bad pynkmen ia ki nongwan sngap ki nongpyniaid jong kane ka Concert ki la rai ban ym shim kano kano ka bairung bad ki lah ban siew “Katkum Ka Jingkwah Jong Nongwan Sngap" Kane ka Concert kan long ha Dorbar Hall Cum Indoor Stadium Mission Compound, Shillong haka 9 tarik une ubnai Rymphang.

Ban shu ia rwai"Ri Khasi Ri Khasi, Nga ieid ïa pha"khlem ka jingïatylli ka long lehnohei katba ka ‘Jaidbynriew’ ka don ha thmier u riat, u la bynrap.
U Bah Nongtraw la ong shuh shuh ba ka shong ha ki paidbah mynta hato ki kwah ban ïohi ia ka jingkylla ne ki kwah ban shah teh shah khum bad ka la por ba ka la dei mynta ban iatreilang kum kawei sur na bynta ka bha ka miat jong ka lawei jong ka jaidbynriew Hynniewtrep.
U la ong ba ka Council kam long pyrshah ia kano kano ka jaidbynriew ne jait niam hynrei ban iada ia ka jaidbynriew Hynniewtrep na ki jingthmu basniew jong ka India te kumta banse kim hap ban kieng aktiar.
Ha kawei pat ka liang, ka HNLC ka la pynlong ia ka jingialang jong ka central executive committee ha 2 tarik u bnai Kyllalyngkot mynta u snem ha Krem Tirot haba ki la jied ia u Bah Bobby Marwein kum u Chairman cum Commander-in-Chief bad U Bah Nongtraw yn bat ïa ka shuki General Secretary bad kumjuh ruh kum u Publicity Secretary.
Kiwei pat ki nongialam ki long u Bah Khrawbok Jyrwa kum Vice Chairman, Alex Diengdoh kum Foreign Secretary, Wanshan Marwein kum Finance Secretary, Riewpyrkhat Sun kum Organising Secretary bad M Rynjah kum Socio Cultural Secretary.
JOWAI: Haduh ka sngi kaba lai jong ka jingthep jinglong kyrtong ne nomination na bynta ban ïakhun ïa ka elekshon sha ka ïing dorbar thawain jong ka Jaiñtia Hills Autonomous District Council (JHADC) tang shiphew ngut kiba dang thep kyrteng na bynta ki 29 tylli ki shuki ba thylli.

Haba mih ki jingpynbna lait kam lait jam ha DSC ne MPSC tang na bynta kawei ka post kaba ioh tulop  hapoh 30000 ruh da ki spah ne hajar ngut ki samla ki wan shakhmat ban thep kam haba kin hap ban ialeh ia ki eskamin bapher bapher ban ioh ia ka kam.

JOWAI: U Ma Lakhon Biam, u engineer uba la ïehnoh ïa kam bad uba shah rem haka elekshon MLA 2018 ula ong “Nga la rung sha jylli ka saiñ hima sima ba ngan ïoh shna aiñ bad ban shakri uba duk ba rangli namar ba bun ki jingmyntoi ba ki paidah ki dei ban ïoh ym shym la pynpoi hok sha u paidbah".
“Ka kam nongmihkhmat ka dei ka kam kaba khia bad u nongmihkhmat u dei ban long u briew uba ïohi jngai bad ban don ka mission kumjuh ban ïasaid ïaka ïap ka im u paidbah, hynrei kumba jia long u nongmihkhmat ba phi la jied na kane ka thain u shong khop hapoh ka ïing dorbar ka JHADC la 15 snem kynthih", la ong u Ma Lakhon Biam u kyrtong ka United Democratic Party (UDP) na Nongbah haba kren haka jingïalang ban pan jingkyrshan jong u paidbah haka sngi Thohdieng.
Une u kyrtong ka UDP un aireng para marwei pyrshah ïa u kyrtong ka National People’s Party (NPP) u Ma Shemhok Garod uba long u MDC ba mynta.
Haba kren shuh shuh u ma Lakhon ula ong ba ula rai ban ïakhun elekshon MDC hadien ka jingïasyllok bad ki riew rangbah ka thaiñ bad ki nongkyrshan ba radbah ka party UDP.
La pdiang burom ïa u ma Lakhon ha u Nohprah 18 bad la jied ruh ïa u ban long u President ka UDP Raliang LA Constituency.
“Lada phi jied ïa nga, ngan ïasaid naka bynta jong phi bad ban thaw ïaki aiñ kiban ïada ïaka riti ka dustur bad ka jaidbynriew katkum bala pynkup bor haka sixth schedule", la ong u ma Lakhon bad kynthoh ïaka jingai trading license pathar ka JHADC ïa u bar jylla wat ha ki kam ba u trai ri u lah ban trei.
Ha kane ka sngi la jied ruh ïaki nongkitkam ka UDP ha 7 Nongbah MDC Constituency.
U President u Eborlang Dhar, Vice President Conboyry Hinge, Secretary Comfort Thubru, Assistant Secretary Lakhon Phawa, Treasurer Phaimi Biam And 26 Executive Members.
Haka Women Wing la jied President ïaka Tipsngi Songwai, Vice President Loyal Sungoh, Secretary Momtis Thubru, Treasurer Jukimon Hinge bad 24 Members.
Iaka jingïalang la pynïaid da u ma Raplang Lamare.
JOWAI: U Myntri Rangbah ka Jylla u Conrad Kongkal Sangma ula wan ban plie ïaka website jong ka Krangshuri Adventure Tours haka sngi Palei.
Ha kane ka jingplie ïaka website ka Krangshuri la ïadonlang u Ma Lahkmen Rymbui MLA ka War Jaiñtia, u ma Sniawbhalang Dhar Myntri C&RD ka sorkar Jylla bad u DC, SP West Jaiñtia Hills District bad kiwei kiwei ki ophisar jong ka tnad treikam bapher bapher.
La ïadonlang ki nongïalam ka Raid Buam & Environmental Protection Association ba kynthup ïa u Donbok Buam, uba maitphang ban pynbha ïaka Krangshuri badn khring ïaki nongwan jngohkai na kylleng.
U Sangma haba kren kum u kongsan ula ong ba u kmen ban pynbna ba ka sorkar pdeng kala theh T.200 klur ban kyntiew ïaka kam jngohkai.
“T.22 klur tang ha West Jaiñtia Hills Disrtict ban kyntiew ïaka jingïalehkai hapoh um (water sports) ha Iooksi T.10.87, T.7.34 Klur ïaka’law kyntang ka Chyrmang ban ïada ïaki jingthaw ba im bad pynlong ïaka kum kawei na ki jaka shangkai pyrthei".
“Ban pynbha ïaka Kranshuri la mang T.3.19 Klur ban shna shurok, dukan dih sha bad kiwei kiwei", la ong u Conrad.
U MLA ka thaiñ ula ong “ban kyntiew ïaka kam jngohkai ngin dei ban pynneh pynsah ïaki khlaw ki btab kiba lah ban pynmih ïaka um ka wah bad lada ym don dieng ka mut ym don ki kshaid kiba noh rymphum.
Ban kyntiew ïaka kam jngohkai ngi dei ban tyngkai ïaka jingai ka mariang bad ban pynlong ïaki shnong ki thaw kiba khuid ba suba".
Ha kane ka sngi la pynkup burom ïa ki samla ïalehkai ban kiew shakhmat haka jingim ïalehkai footbal ka Lajong bad u Donbok Buam u seng kam lajong.
JOWAI: U Conrad Kongkal Sangma Myntri Rangbah ka Jylla ula kren kop ba ka heh ka ïarong pisa ban kyntiew ïaka kam jngohkai pyrthei haka Jylla.
U Conrad ula ong ba ka sorkar pdeng kala theh T.200 klur ban kyntiew bad ban pynbha ïaki kam jngohkai haka jylla baroh kawei.
“Tang ka West Jaiñtia Hills ban kyntiew ïaki jaka jngohkai jong ka ka sorkar jylla kala ai bhah T.22 klur ban pynbha ïaki jaka jngohkai", la ong u Conrad haba kren haka jingïalang plie ïaka jaka jngohkai ka shnong Kudengrim haka sngi Palei.
Ka Kudengrim, ka dei ka shong kaba jngai tang 25 KM na Amlarem bad 50 na Jowai ka don ka jingkieng jri ba ar mala bad ki shi mala kaba la shna pynbha da ki nongshong shnong, ka don ka kshaid kaba itynnad ha ka wah Amlamar, ki ïing skhen ban peit kai bad ki lynti ïaid kjat da ki skhen ban poi sha ka kshaid Amlamar.
Ka don ruh ki lynti ïaid kjat bala oh shrong da ki maw bad ki jinghkieng doi doi ki bad kiwei kiwei.
Ki samla shnong bad ki nongïalam shnong ka shong Kudengrim naduh mynshem snem ha u Naiwieng kila pynsaphriang ïaka khubor lyngba ki lad pathai khubor ‘social media’ halor ka jingitynnad ka jaka bad kala khring ïa kiba ba bun ban wan shangkai sha katei ka shnong; kaba nakaliang u Conrad ula ïaroh bad ula pynshlur ba kane ka dei ka buit ban saphriang ïaki jingdon ka jaka shangkai sha ka pyrthei.
Hadien bala thaw ïaka Kudengrim Tourism and Environmental Protection Society (KTEPS), ki samla bad rangbah kila sdang ban shna jingkieng jri bad ki lynti ban poi sha ka kshaid Amlamar da ki siej.
U Conrad Sangma ula ong ba ka sorkar MDA kala shimkhia bha ban kyntiew ïaka kam jngohkai pyrthei  bad ula ong “Shen ka shnong jong phi kan ïoh ka surok ban pynïasoh bad ka Sohkha, Dawki bad kiwei ki shnong ba marjan ban khring ïa ki nongwan shangkai".
“Phi dei ban lah ban khring ïa ki nongwan kai na ri thor na Bangladesh bad ban pynsah kham bun sngi sha kane ka jaka ba ngi pylut por haka dih ka bam kum ka kyiad, kaba ri Bangladesh ka dei ka ri tyrkhong Kyiad", la ong u Conrad.
“Ka kam jngohkai ka dei kawei na ki lad ban kamai jakpoh, phi dei ban trei shitom ban pynneh pynsah  ïaka jingitynnad ka mariang bad wat shna kino kino ki jintei ban pynjulor ïaka jingitynnad ", ong u Myntri Rangbah ka Jylla.
SHILLONG: Ki paidbah kiba wan sha ka jingialang bala pynlong da ka Khasi Students Union ki la risa jam ha ka por ba ai jingkren u MLA na Nongkrem Konstituensi u Bah Lambor Malngiang uba la ther tyngeh ia BJP Sorkar da kaba ong “Sala Sorkar BJP.
U la ong shuh shuh ha ka por ba ki leit iakynduh ia Home Minister jong ka Sorkar Kmie U Rajnath Singh ki khlem Namaste ne ai khublei ia u, hynrei ki la shu ong ia pyndam noh ia ka Citizenship Amendment Bill (CAB), 2016.
Kumban shu pynkynmaw hangne ba ia ka sorkar Meghalaya Democratic Alliance la thaw lang da ka NPP, ka BJP, ka UDP bad kiwei kiwei de ki parti bad MLA shimet.
